Detailed Report on the Chongming Typhoon Disaster 88

Over 400 Deaths, Extensive Damage

Chongming Island is located at the mouth of the Yangtze River, close to Sheshan Mountain, and therefore suffered the most from the recent hurricane. On the evening of the second, the hurricane blew southwest, causing seawater to flow back into the Yangtze River. It also coincided with the high tide on the 13th day of the lunar calendar, causing the river tide to rise sharply by over a zhang. The fierce waves poured like mountains, surrounding the sea, and all the embankments were breached. The entire county, except for the city walls and the high ground in the center, was submerged, with water depths ranging from two or three chi to over a zhang. Although the water has receded within the county, the coastal areas are still flooded due to the breaches in the embankments. According to investigations, the number of people drowned has already exceeded 400, with the number of missing still difficult to count. Corpses are found everywhere, a truly tragic sight. The fifth district, which mainly produces grain and corn, had already harvested its crops and stored them at home, but they were either washed away or submerged. The losses are enormous. Countless houses were washed away or collapsed, leaving countless people homeless and in need of food. Party and government authorities and citizens such as Wang Qingmu have sent telegrams to higher authorities and charitable organizations in Shanghai, requesting urgent relief. Detailed reports on the affected areas are as follows: District 1: Dozens of houses collapsed in the southern area near the city, and crops were damaged, but there were no fatalities. In Hongqiao Town in the north, the embankments were completely destroyed, and the water level was six chi above ground, destroying over 60 houses and drowning five elderly people and children. The entire town of Beipaiyazhen was washed away, with over 60 houses collapsing and over ten people, including Wu Shanqing, dying. Meijiahe was already prone to landslides and had the most dangerous terrain. That night, the tide reached over a zhang above ground level. Fortunately, residents along the coast had evacuated in advance, but over 100 thatched and tiled houses were washed away or collapsed, and over 20 villagers were killed or injured. District 2: In the northern part of Bangzhen, west of places like Miaogang and Zhangwanggang, the embankments completely collapsed, with over 200 houses collapsing and as many as 50 villagers drowning. The entire Yonghe Yuhuangsha sandbar was submerged, and the water has not yet receded, making it impossible to estimate the extent of the damage. In Nansha, nine out of ten embankments were breached, and over 60 thatched houses were washed away. However, villagers, mindful of the 1920 flood, had evacuated to higher ground in advance and were not drowned. District 3: The thatched houses in the boundaries of the Eighth Map were all blown away. The water level in the northern part of Dachunzhen was six chi high, killing or injuring six or seven people and destroying over ten houses. In the villages of Zhuchun, Xiezhi, and Dongxiang Tongtadun, corpses were seen everywhere, a sight too painful to describe. It is estimated that over a hundred people drowned. The water level in various places is still over four chi high, and the losses are enormous, making it impossible to estimate for the time being. District 4: In the northern and southern forts, 19 power lines and poles were broken. The northern coast suffered less damage. In the northern coastal town of Hexingzhen, the east-west embankments were breached by the tide, collapsing over 100 houses and drowning 60 to 70 villagers. District 5: Located in the eastern corner, the terrain is low-lying, and the embankments are soft, making it particularly vulnerable to disaster. In the northern coastal villages, such as Jingze, Yusheng, and Caomiao, over 20 embankments were breached, with water depths exceeding one zhang, drowning over a hundred men and women. Crops such as flowers, grains, and beans were completely submerged and rotted. Thatched houses were completely destroyed, and nine out of ten tiled houses collapsed. The floodwater is still four or five chi deep, leaving the survivors displaced, exposed to the elements, and starving. District 6: The terrain is relatively high, but the water level in both the north and south coasts reached three or four chi. The embankments outside Wananzhen were breached, destroying over ten thatched houses and drowning seven or eight people. District 7: The disaster affected over one-third of the entire district, with the northeastern coast of Mengjiangmiao being the most severely affected. The water depth was over five chi, and thatched and tiled houses were submerged and destroyed everywhere. In the area of Dalongsha, several embankments were breached. The official embankments of Men'an, Liangzi, Xingzi, Xizi, and Zizu, as well as the northwestern coast of Haihongzhen, were all breached, turning the area into a vast swamp. Fortunately, villagers evacuated early, and only over 30 people were crushed or drowned. However, a large amount of rice, miscellaneous items, and livestock were washed into the sea, resulting in massive losses. In the county's Shengshan fishing area, over 100 houses were destroyed that night, and around 300 fishing boats were smashed and sunk. The number of fishermen killed is impossible to count. Two-thirds of the fishermen have lost their homes and are facing starvation. Party and government authorities have hired ships and sent personnel to provide relief. There was also much loss in Sijing, Daji, Xiaoji, and other mountains, but the details are unknown.

Mei Yilin Inspects the Flood Situation on the North Bank of the Yellow River 89

=After arriving in Shouzhang, he convened the county magistrates for consultation=

=Returned to Jinan and then went to Henan to inspect the affected areas=

Jinan Correspondence: This time, the Yellow River breached its banks in Hebei and Henan, flooding twenty counties and affecting millions of people. The situation is extremely dire. The central government, in order to coordinate relief efforts, specially appointed Mei Yilin as the disaster investigation commissioner, who went to Shandong, Henan, and Hebei provinces to inspect the affected areas. After arriving in Shandong, Mei first went from Yanzhou to Jining and then to Xiangcheng, Yutai, Jiaxiang, and Jinxiang. On the evening of the eighth, he arrived in Jinan from the affected areas. On the morning of the ninth, he went to Luokou again, and inspected the affected areas along the north bank of the Yellow River to Shouzhang. He also convened the county magistrates of Puxian, Fanxian, Dong'a, Shouzhang, and Yanggu to inquire about the disaster situation. Today (the tenth) at 2:00 PM, he returned to Jinan from the north bank. At 9:10 PM that evening, he took the Pinghu train to Xuzhou and then went to Lanfeng and Kaocheng in Henan.

When Mr. Mei went to the north bank of the Yellow River to investigate the disaster, he departed by special train at 8:00 AM on the morning of the ninth. At 8:15 AM, the special train crossed the Luokou Yellow River Railway Bridge, seeing that the Yellow River had receded significantly, but the flow was still strong. Originally, it was planned to change to a car on the north bank of Luokou, but because the Yellow River mud was everywhere after the river receded, it was inconvenient to walk, so the special train went north again. At 8:40 AM, it arrived at the Sangzidian Station, where it changed to a car and proceeded westward. There were four long-distance cars prepared by the Department of Construction, and one private car of Li Shuchun, which Mei, Li, and Xin shared. The remaining four cars were shared by the accompanying personnel. At 1:00 PM, it arrived at the Xiangshan car station, got off the car to rest briefly, and had lunch. After lunch, it got on the car again and proceeded. At 2:00 PM, it passed Taochengbu, and at 4:00 PM, it arrived at Shouzhang County. When passing Taochengbu, the overflowing water was seen from a distance, still rushing into the Yellow River, the current was still very rapid, and the previous situation could be imagined. Continuing westward, south of the Jin embankment and north of the river, there was a vast expanse of water without any boundaries. All villages and fields were completely submerged. What could be seen were only a few rooftops and treetops floating on the water. It is said that the current water level has significantly decreased, and before it decreased, it could be imagined. Even now, the water depth is still more than one zhang. The lives of the victims are truly unbearable. Except for those who were drowned and washed away without any trace and cannot be proven, according to what can be seen now, the rooftops and mountain peaks have become the victims' happy nests, exposing them to the night dew, crying from hunger and cold, and the sounds can be heard in the fields. Everywhere one looks, there are scenes of property being destroyed and families scattered, which cannot be counted. The daily lives of the victims are mostly filled with eating leaves and bark. When one hears that relief is being distributed, it is like a drop in the bucket, not enough to help. They can only eat their fill once and then go hungry all day long. This situation is truly unbearable and cannot be described in words.

After arriving in Shouzhang, the county magistrate Zhuang Shouchong led the county government and various agencies, representatives of the victims, and Yang Jifeng, the county magistrate of Yanggu, An Maolong, the county magistrate of Dong'a, and Zhou Junying, the county magistrate of Fanxian, because they received a telegram from Li Shuchun, the head of the Department of People's Affairs, from Jining, and rushed to Shouzhang to greet them. The county magistrate of Puxian was unable to arrive due to an emergency. Mei, Li, Xin, and others got off the car outside the city, walked into the city with the county magistrates, and went to the county government. After a brief rest, Mei immediately inquired about the disaster situation from the county magistrates. According to the report of Zhuang Shouchong, the county magistrate of Shouzhang, the county has ten districts, all of which have been affected by the disaster. A total of over 600 hectares in the five districts on the south bank were flooded, with more than 90 villages and over 4,800 households, affecting over 25,000 people. On the north bank, more than 2,300 hectares in the five districts were flooded, affecting more than 290 villages, over 15,600 households, and over 81,000 people, with losses of more than 54 million yuan. In total, all ten districts of the county were flooded with more than 2,900 hectares, affecting 385 villages, more than 20,400 households, and over 106,000 people, with losses of more than 6.4 million yuan. He continued, saying that the water in the county, after the Yellow River breached its banks at Erfenzhuang in Hebei Province, flowed into the Qingshui River and Ji River, which run through the sixth and eighth districts of the county, and spread in all directions, flooding all the fields and crops. Countless houses collapsed, and fertile land was turned into a swamp. It was found that the two rivers came from Yuncheng and entered Dongping Lake through Guanxian. Therefore, the disaster was lighter in previous years, but now the lakeshore along Dongping has been built into a dam, and the water coming from the south cannot enter the lake and cannot be discharged, resulting in flooding and the development of a disaster area. To this day, the water level is still rising, and there is no hope of sowing wheat. The victims have all fled, and the severity of the disaster in the future is unknown. Then, An Maolong, the county magistrate of Dong'a, reported that 42 townships in the county were flooded, a total of 203 villages, affecting 11,866 households and 71,334 people, flooding 2,422.1007 hectares of land. The water depth in all the flooded areas was 7 or 8 chi. The victims did not plant wheat last year, and this year's autumn harvest was also flooded. There is a shortage of food, and the victims are all crying out for food. Although the Provincial Relief Committee has provided relief, it is only a drop in the bucket and does not solve the problem. Please provide relief as soon as possible. Next, Yang Jifeng, the county magistrate of Yanggu, reported that one-quarter of the county was flooded, a total of 3, 5, 6, and 3 districts. The third district has more than 3,400 victims, 40 hectares of flooded land, countless houses collapsed, and losses of more than 35,000 yuan. The fifth district has more than 2,000 victims, more than 500 hectares of flooded land, more than 3,000 houses, and losses of more than 77 million yuan. The sixth district has more than 18,000 victims, more than 100 hectares of flooded land, more than 4,000 houses, and losses of more than 600,000 yuan. Then, Zhou Junying, the county magistrate of Fanxian, reported that the first district of the county was flooded with 820 hectares of land, 75 villages, a total of 2,220 households, affecting 15,320 people (one death), with losses of about 1.2 million yuan. The third district was flooded with 600 hectares of land, 63 villages, a total of 2,100 households, affecting 14,830 people (two deaths), with losses of about 900,000 yuan. The third district was flooded with 420 hectares of land, 45 villages, a total of 1,090 households, affecting 13,710 people (three deaths). The fourth district was flooded with 1,600 hectares of land, 257 villages, a total of 4,300 households, affecting 49,310 people (six deaths), with losses of 1.6 million yuan. In total, 340 villages, 10,052 households, and a total of 93,171 victims were affected, with 13 deaths and losses of more than 4.5 million yuan.

The representatives of the victims in Shouzhang County, Ma Guishan, Shi Xingmo, Sun Baoshan, Chen Xixian, Tan Xuekong, Cao Yalin, Tong Xianzhang, Meng Guangrong, Yue Shuxun, Yuan Dianyuan, Li Yantian, Yue Chongjue, Jiang Zunhui, and Liu Xiqin, wrote a letter to Mr. Mei at the county government, stating, "Since the Yellow River breached its banks at Shitouzhuan in Changyuan County, Hebei Province, the water flowed eastward with great force. The county is low-lying and is located in its path. In a few days, the water depth reached from one zhang to four zhang. The number of people and livestock washed away is countless. The affected area in the county stretches 80 li diagonally from east to west and 30 li to 40 li from north to south, covering 280 villages with a population of approximately 120,000 and an area of more than 2,700 hectares. The estimated losses in the affected area are approximately 2 million yuan for fields and crops, 1.4 million yuan for collapsed houses, and over 2 million yuan for washed-away livestock and other property. The total losses on the north bank of the county are more than 5.4 million yuan. In addition, the south bank of the county has also suffered from floods. One area, from Huanghuasi to the south to Yezhuzhao, is 40 li long and 7 or 8 li wide from east to west, covering more than 50 villages, which have all been submerged. The other area, since the Erfenzhuang breach in Dongming, the water from Heze and Yuncheng flows into the Qingshui River in the territory of Shouzhang at Zhao Jiaba, flooding in all directions and submerging more than 30 villages, about 50 li long and 5 or 6 li to 10 li wide, becoming a vast expanse of water. The third area, the Yellow River water level rose and overflowed, submerging the villages along the river, about 40 li long. The losses from the flood on the south bank of the county are also estimated to be more than 1 million yuan. The total losses from the floods on the north and south banks are more than 6.4 million yuan. The facts of the floods and the amount of losses in the county are hereby presented for your review and forwarding. We also request that you provide relief and close the breach as soon as possible to help the victims. We are grateful and await your orders."

At 5:00 PM, after Mr. Mei had completed the county magistrates' reports on the disaster situation, he went to the streets to inspect everything. Accompanied by Xin Zhujiu, the Standing Committee of the Provincial Relief Committee, and Huang, the secretary of the Shouzhang County Government, who acted as a guide, he first visited the prison and then the streets. Mr. Mei asked the peddlers about the prices of goods and the local people's livelihood. At 7:00 PM, Mr. Mei and the county magistrates went to the county's first elementary school for dinner. That night, all the disaster investigators stayed at the school. Mr. Mei, having received reports from the county magistrates about the disaster situation, returned to Jinan on the tenth. In the morning, after a light breakfast, he left Shouzhang by car at 5:30 AM. At 1:05 PM, he arrived in Jinan. At 3:00 PM, he met with Han Fuqu at the provincial government. Mr. Mei told people that the disaster situation in Shandong was very serious and had been reported to the central government. He would take the train to Xuzhou and then to Kaifeng to investigate the disaster situation that night (the tenth) at 9:10 PM. (Tenth)

The People of Xiaodang Oppose Blocking the Dasha River Mouth 90

Fengpei Counties Have Sent Teams to Measure and Estimate the Work

Xiaodang Representatives Petition the Jiangsu Provincial Government to Stop It

Xuzhou Correspondence: Last month, the Yellow River water from eastern Henan entered Xuzhou and flowed eastward along the old channel. When it reached Gaozhai on the eastern border of Dangshan, it turned north into the Dasha River, flowing backward into Fengpei to enter Zhaoyang and Weishan Lakes. Therefore, the amount of water flowing eastward along the old channel was reduced. In addition, with the obstruction of the Erba dams, Xiaotong was not affected by the floods. Therefore, the four counties of Fengpei, Xiaodang are in a conflicting position of interests regarding the Yellow River water. The counties of Tong, Pi, Sui, and Su are behind them. If the Yellow River water flows eastward from the old channel by breaching the Erba dams, it must pass through eastern Dangshan and northern Xiao before reaching the territory of Tong, and only after passing through Tong can it reach Pi, Sui, and Su again. If it completely enters Weishan Lake from the Dasha River, it must enter the canal from the river to reach Pi and Su counties. The Jingshan and Bulao Rivers in Tongshan, which are connected to Weishan Lake, must overflow to the south for the lake water to flow into them. Now, people in Fengpei, suffering from the floods of the Yellow River, intend to block the mouth of the Dasha River to restrain the flow of water to the north, while simultaneously dredging and releasing the Erba dams so that the Yellow River water still flows eastward along the old channel. In this way, Fengpei can be guaranteed safety. Teams have already been sent to the Dasha River mouth and the Erba dam area to measure and estimate the work. People in Xiaodang were alarmed upon hearing the news. Because the old Yellow River has been silted up for a long time, the Dasha River is the path the Yellow River took when it breached its banks and flowed north in the past. The riverbed is particularly lower than the old Yellow River. Forcibly blocking the low-lying river mouth and opening the high-lying dams is somewhat akin to shifting the water to harm others. Furthermore, if the water flows north from the Dasha River, there is still Weishan Lake to store it. If it flows eastward along the old channel, it will inevitably overflow and have nowhere to return. Therefore, not only can the Erba dams not be opened, but the Dasha River mouth cannot be forcibly blocked. As a result, they concentrated their efforts to defend the Erba dams and sent representatives to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the Xuzhou Garrison Headquarters, and the Commissioner's Office of the Twelfth District to request that they be ordered to stop it. Upon receiving the petition, Commissioner She Nianci believed that the dredging and blocking of waterways was related to the entire district and that it was necessary to coordinate to avoid disputes. He immediately ordered Yang Liang, the county magistrate of Fengxian, and Hu Zhaohe, the county magistrate of Peixian, to prohibit the people from blocking the mouth of the Dasha River and wait for the report to be submitted to the provincial government for review and handling. The people of Fengpei, believing that the Gaozhai and Erba dams were all within the territory of Dangshan, could not meddle in the affairs of others with the strength of the two counties alone. Therefore, they invited people from Dangyi to a meeting in Fengxian. People from Dangyi refused to go, believing that if the Erba dams were dredged and released, the eastern districts of Dangdong would inevitably suffer from floods, followed by Xiaotong. They contacted people in northern Xiao, who in turn contacted people in eastern Tong, and unanimously advocated opposition. The people along the Binhe River in Dangxiao, hearing that the people of Fengpei were preparing to block the river mouth and breach the dams with armed force, were also alarmed and gathered armed forces to defend themselves, prepared to fight to the death. Commissioner She, believing that the location of the dispute between the four counties was all in Dangshan, immediately sent personnel to Dangshan to investigate and strictly ordered the counties to avoid disputes and await a coordinated solution. If the Yellow River were to change its course, there would be no reason to return to the old channel in the Xuzhou area. The old channel has been silted up for a long time and is much higher than other fields. This time, the flooding in the Xuzhou area was caused by the breach and overflow of the river. Preventing breaches and floods is fundamentally linked to the closure of the breaches in western Henan and Shandong. The flood control of each county is a temporary measure. The fundamental water conservancy problem in peacetime is still to dredge the rivers so that each river flows smoothly and storage and discharge are appropriate, which is enough to eliminate floods and develop water conservancy. Attached is the petition of the representatives of Xiaodang, "We present this to prevent people from harming others, gathering crowds to demonstrate, and the situation is urgent. We hope you will review and quickly stop it to avoid bloodshed and relieve the people. We secretly investigated that in the first year of Xianfeng of the Qing Dynasty, the north bank of the Yellow River collapsed in Dangjing Panlongji, pouring into Fengpei (the people of Fengpei commonly call it the Dasha River) Nanyang Zhaoyang Weishan lakes. At that time, the flood was torrential, and the riverbed was more than twelve li wide. The old Yellow River was turned over because of the accumulation of abandoned sand, which was more than one zhang higher than the newly rushed riverbed in Fengpei. There are Erba dams and Ying Shui dams in the east, and the terrain is even higher. Therefore, this time the Yellow River flooded to Panlongji east of Gaozhai, and still followed the old road of Fengpei into the lake. Water nature takes the lower place, and the terrain makes it. However, the people of Fengpei have come up with a strange idea, wanting to move the water that is lower and put it on the stop. Yesterday, they actually took a survey team of several people and two or thirty police officers, from Dangjing, along the Panlongji, and along the Erba dams to conduct on-site surveys, allocating 20,000 low-ranking workers to build dams to block the river mouth entering Fengpei, and to open the Ying Shui dam south of the Erba dam to allow the flooded Yellow River water to be introduced into the territory of Xiaotong to avoid harming Fengpei. It is also proposed to station the police groups of the two counties such as Ji, with 10,000 guns, to be stationed for security south of the Erba dams in Dangjing. It is also proposed to set up a construction supervision office in Gaozhai, install telephones, and lay electric lights, and construction will begin soon. The villages heard the news, running and sweating, indignant. Moreover, since the Yellow River moved north, the riverbed has become fertile land, and the national treasury is not owed any silk or grain. Villages and towns are lined up along the river, such as Tangzhai in Dangzhai, Huangkou, Laongji, Haozhai in Xiao, Tongshan County Town, Xuzhou Commercial Port, and the two stations of Jinpu Longhai, all located on the south bank of the old Yellow River. If this water transfer plan of Fengpei is successful, all important cities and towns and transportation routes will be in turmoil and shock every day. As for the riverbed entering Fengpei, the terrain is low-lying, the riverbed is wide and deep, and the water coming from the upper reaches goes straight to the lakes, like a waterfall, and does not harm the fields, villages, and towns. This is evident from the fact that the Yellow River water flows north into Fengpei and does not flow south into Xiaotong. However, the people of Fengpei insist on making the water that does no harm to themselves harmful to others. The representatives cannot understand this. In order to protect their lives and property, the people can only wait with weapons, just waiting for a firefight. In addition to the public presentation, we hereby present the facts. We hope that you will quickly stop the bloodshed and relieve the people. We are eagerly waiting for your orders." (September 11)

Nanchang Airport Groundbreaking Ceremony 91

Xiong Shihui Leads Public Officials to Work

Nanchang Correspondence: The Nanchang Airport today (September 11) held a groundbreaking ceremony. Officials from the Commander-in-Chief's Camp, the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and its affiliated agencies, as well as staff members from various public organizations in Nanchang City, participated in the ceremony. The rostrum was set up at the southeast end of the airport, with a horizontal banner made of white bamboo cloth with the words "Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Construction of Nanchang Airport by All Circles of the Jiangxi Provincial Capital in Cooperation with the Suppression of Bandits." At around 8:00 AM, Qin Le opened the meeting, and Xiong Shihui served as the chairman. He first reported on the significance of the meeting, stating that the Red bandits are a fatal wound to the nation's lifeline, and the men, women, old, and young of the province have suffered terribly from the Red disaster, so they all hope that the Red bandits will be eliminated as soon as possible. However, whether the Red bandits can be eliminated as soon as possible depends on whether our cooperative suppression work to relieve ourselves of our own pain is tense or not. In the military suppression of the Red bandits, the air force accounts for one-third of the strength of the navy and army. The central government has sent a large number of capable aircraft to Gan, and everyone should work together to complete this airfield as soon as possible. Then, Hu Jiayi, the director of the Highway Bureau, reported on the construction methods. After the report, Xiong instructed each agency to assign one person to direct and maintain order during work. Then, led by Xiong Shihui, the staff of each agency, one team after another, carrying the shovels, hoes, baskets, and shoulder poles prepared by the Highway Bureau, went to the side of the small hill next to the venue and worked simultaneously with over ten thousand civilian workers around the area. They dispersed after two hours (September 11).

Suspicious Gunshot Wound to Li Xu Shi 95

At 3:30 AM on the 12th, a gunshot was suddenly heard at the west entrance of Xiaoshu Lane outside Changmen. Police officers on duty rushed to investigate and found Xu Shi, the wife of Li Shuangxi, who lived there, lying injured in front of her door. A bullet had entered her left breast and exited her shoulder, causing a very critical condition. According to Liu Shi, the wife of Lu Sanlong, who lived in a nearby shack, their shack was being repaired, and the couple was leaning against the door when a thief broke in and stole a package of clothing from a wooden box. They chased and caught up with the thief with the help of neighbor Li Silou, but the thief pulled out a pistol and fired before escaping. Li Xu Shi happened to be watching the commotion in front of her door and was hit by a stray bullet. However, the case is highly suspicious because the victim, Lu Sanlong, has no valuable possessions, so why would a thief with a pistol target him? Furthermore, a new leather shoe was left behind. The injured Li Xu Shi has been sent to Gengsheng Hospital, but she is unable to speak due to the severity of her injuries. The responsible Public Security Bureau is investigating the truth.

Wuxi 97

Two Students Disappear Simultaneously

Liu Pingjiang, a native of Yixing County and former county magistrate, resides on the bank in the city. After leaving his official career, he served as the director of general affairs at the Provincial Public Education Institute in Sheqiao, Wuxi. His wife, Mrs. So-and-so, had a son and a daughter. The eldest daughter, Minghuan, is a student at Zhenhua Girls' High School in Suzhou. The son, Xingji, is 18 years old and graduated from the Provincial Normal Junior High School in Wuxi last semester. Mrs. So-and-so passed away a few years ago, and Liu remarried Zhang Sheng, the director of moral education at the Suzhou Women's Normal School. Zhang served as the principal of Jingzhi Girls' School in Wuxi this year. The Liu family's life is extremely comfortable. Xingji is served by servants and enjoys a life of ease. When Xingji was at school, he was admired by teachers and students for his intelligence and wrote many works. However, he had a melancholy and eccentric personality. He believed that going to university would create a class of highly educated idlers, so he took a passive attitude towards subjects he considered unnecessary. However, the school authorities often attached great importance to what Xingji considered unnecessary. Therefore, after graduating last semester, he failed to be admitted to Changzhou High School, Soochow Academy, Suzhou School, and others. He was finally admitted to the Suzhou Art Academy, but his family was very dissatisfied, and Xingji was constantly depressed and unhappy. He spent his days wandering on the park road, pacing in the cinema, or roaming near graveyards, filled with melancholy thoughts. Day after day, his appearance grew haggard, and his mind became distracted. On the afternoon of the 30th of last month, he took his everyday clothes and seven or eight silver dollars for spending money and left home. Upon discovering this, his parents immediately sent telegrams and searched everywhere, but there was no news or trace of him. Liu Pingjiang was heartbroken at the loss of his son in his old age, and his nerves were greatly affected. To their surprise, the day before yesterday, they suddenly discovered that Xingji's best friend, Kong Deyang, had also disappeared at the same time. Kong is from Zhutang Town in Jiangyin. His father, Kong Jinquan, is also from a moderately wealthy family. Yesterday, Kong's elder brother, Kong Dexing, came to Wuxi to search for him after hearing the news, but there was also no trace of him. It is thought that Liu and Kong have embarked on a wandering journey, but it is unknown where they are. Currently, the families of the two students have entrusted people to search in Suzhou, Shanghai, and other places, hoping to find them.

Shangyu 102

The Collapse of the Zhanglu Dike in Songxia Causes Disaster

For nearly a week in this county, there has been incessant high winds and torrential rain. The Cao'e River, swollen by seventy tributaries, has caused the tide to rise and flood to a height of several meters. More than twenty villages along the river, located in low-lying areas, have had their crops and by-products submerged, resulting in substantial losses. The old Qiutang Dike in Zhanglu Village, Songxia, has been in disrepair for years, and the dike body was not strong to begin with. Continued erosion by the raging waves caused it to collapse suddenly a few days ago. The floodwaters inundated more than a thousand acres of sandy land, washing away all the crops planted there. The farmers are all crying out in distress.

Letter to the Editor 103

To the Editor:

I recently read a section in the "Local News" column of your newspaper on the 10th about the Director of the Wuxi Sulfur and Nitrate Bureau being sued, which is not consistent with the facts. I have held this position for a year now, and I have always aimed to balance the interests of the public and businesses. The inspectors I have appointed are only a small number, not excessive. Recently, the production of fireworks by Hui Xuyuan, Gu Rongmao, Xu Yuanmao, and others was suspected of using smuggled nitrate. Nitrate is the raw material for manufacturing dangerous goods, and the government has long explicitly prohibited anyone from privately selling or stockpiling it, with strict regulations. Since I learned that these merchants were suspected of smuggling, I naturally sent inspectors to investigate, but there was no act of searching through boxes and chests. What your newspaper reported is absolutely untrue. As for the Fireworks Industry Association, it should have applied to the bureau, but its letter was in the form of an order, which was unacceptable, so I rejected it as being irregular. My headquarters has now sent Commissioner Wang Zhixiang to Wuxi to investigate the matter thoroughly. Right and wrong will be easily judged. I respectfully request that this letter be published in the "Letter to the Editor" column to clarify the facts. With best wishes, I remain,

Yours sincerely,

Fu Huanzeng, Director of the Wuxi Branch of the Sulfur and Nitrate Bureau.

City News

Three Groups of Commissioners for Yellow River Flood Relief Fly to Inspect the Disaster Area Today 104

Chairman Song Continued to Discuss Relief Measures Yesterday Morning

Xinsheng News Agency reports that Song Ziwen, Chairman of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, convened Zeng Rongpu, Director of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Office and Chief of the General Affairs Group, Xi Dejiong, Director of the Disaster Relief Group, and Edward Anner, Chairman of the China International Famine Relief Commission, at the Finance Department's Shanghai Office on West Ames Road to discuss relief efforts for the flood disaster in Shandong, Henan, and Hebei provinces. At 4:00 PM, Xi Dejiong, Zeng Rongpu, and others continued to discuss disaster relief matters at the association's office on the Bund, No. 6, and dispersed at 5:00 PM. Xi will leave for Hongqiao Airport at 6:00 AM this morning to take a Eurasia Aviation Corporation plane to Beijing. Standing Committee member and Director of the Health Group Liu Ruiheng, and Director of the Work Relief Group Zhou Xiangxian, will board the plane in Beijing.

Departing This Morning 105

Central News Agency reports that the Yellow River Flood Disaster Area Situation Committee, in order to understand the actual situation in the disaster area, has appointed Xi Dejiong, Director of the Disaster Relief Group, Zhou Xiangxian, Director of the Work Relief Group, Liu Ruiheng, Director of the Health Group, and a foreign relief expert to inspect the disaster area. Yesterday morning, Xi Dejiong told a Central News Agency reporter:

"Our committee has chartered a plane from Eurasia Aviation Corporation to inspect the disaster area. I will leave Shanghai for Beijing at 6:00 AM tomorrow (the 13th). After a short stay in Beijing, I will fly to the Jinan area with Directors Liu and Zhou, who are currently in Beijing, and a foreign expert to inspect the area. We have decided to stay in Jinan for one day. The next morning, we will fly from Jinan to the Kaifeng area to inspect the area. We will contact local authorities along the way to discuss relief matters. The scheduled trip will be four days." Li Jingcong, General Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, said that the plane chartered by the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee is scheduled to leave Shanghai for Beijing at 6:00 AM tomorrow and fly from Beijing to Jinan at 8:00 AM. The itinerary will be determined after arriving in Jinan.

Scheduled Itinerary 106

At 8:00 AM, fly north from Beijing, detouring through Tongshan, Fengxian, Pei County, Jiaxiang, Dancheng, Juye, Shouzhang, Yanggu, and other counties to inspect the flood situation and disaster conditions. They will also lead technicians from the Army Survey Bureau and Western experts to take photographs along the way. In the afternoon, they will arrive in Jinan to discuss relief matters with local authorities. Tomorrow (the 14th), they will fly south from Jinan, passing through Pu County, Heze, and the disaster areas of Hebei Province, and arrive in Kaifeng to discuss relief efforts with the Henan provincial authorities. The day after tomorrow (the 15th), they will take off from Kaifeng, first inspect the Bianxi and Xingze counties, then fly east, passing through Chenliu, Lanfeng, and Kaocheng, and return to Beijing.

Government Appropriation 107

A reporter from the Guowen News Agency interviewed Zeng Rongpu, Director of the General Affairs Office of the committee, yesterday. According to Zeng, the Yellow River flood has affected almost four provinces: Henan, Shandong, Hebei, and Jiangsu. The Yellow River Relief Committee has been established, and the internal organization is largely in place. The government has allocated four million yuan for expenses. However, everything still needs to await a thorough investigation of the disaster area before detailed statistics are compiled and submitted to the government for approval. Whether this is sufficient or not is difficult to determine at this time. The Shanghai office is located in the National Economic Council on the Bund.

Area Affected by Flooding 108

Subsequently, Li, Director of the Technical Group of the Engineering Department of the Economic Council, said that he saw a report in the newspaper today that the Yellow River Conservancy Commission had entrusted the Aviation Survey Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters to conduct an aerial survey. As a result:

The area affected by the Yellow River flood is 6 million square meters. However, the area we obtained is 34,432 square kilometers, including 6,720 square kilometers in Henan Province, 12,160 square kilometers in Hebei Province, 14,562 square kilometers in Shandong Province, and Jiangsu, which is relatively small, with 990 square kilometers. The area affected by the Yellow River flood this time is indeed very extensive, unprecedented in decades. However, the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee is already planning relief efforts. Relief will be handled by the Disaster Relief Group, while the construction of dikes and dams along the river will be handled by the Work Relief Group. Director Xi and others will fly to the disaster area for inspection tomorrow (today).

The Cause of the Yellow River Disaster 109

Zhu Yong, Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Engineering Department, said that Director Xi (Dejiong) and others will inspect the disaster area, first going to Jinan, as it is very convenient to go from there to Henan and Hebei. The Yangtze River flood this year did not cause a disaster, entirely due to the dike construction and heightening carried out by the Economic Council after the great flood of 1931. Otherwise, this year's flood, although not as extensive as the devastation of 1931, would have turned at least dozens of counties in the provinces along the river, such as Jiangxi and Hubei, into swamps. As for the cause of the Yellow River flood this time, it was due to the high water level in the lower reaches and the siltation in the middle reaches, so the upper reaches, once the water arrived, had no way to discharge it, resulting in a breach. Furthermore, the breach in Lanfeng was originally the entrance to the silted Yellow River. A dam was built there before, but this time, the breach was unable to be stopped by the dam, and it was washed away, causing the Yellow River's water to flood the provinces of Jiangsu and Shandong along the old course. Director Xi's inspection of the disaster area will be quick, probably completed and returned in at most a week. Director Xi is responsible for disaster relief, such as relief, accommodation, and setting up porridge kitchens. The preparation of 100,000 sets of cotton clothes is the responsibility of the General Affairs Group, but I am not aware of the details. The Henan Supervision Office of our department was established earlier. After the Yellow River disaster occurred, our department sent two engineers, Tang Shangsong and Zhang Chongji, to assist in the rescue.

French Concession Authorities Ban Anti-War Congress from Meeting 111

Malais Refutes Japanese Newspaper's News

The China Press reports that the French Concession authorities have refused to allow the Anti-War Congress to be held in the Concession. The French Consul-General, Meyer, yesterday (the 11th) replied to Lord Marley, stating that all political gatherings within the French Concession, regardless of their nature, are prohibited. Therefore, Lord Marley is now requesting the authorities of the International Settlement to allow him to hold a meeting within the Settlement. As for the attitude of the National Government in Nanjing, according to Marley, it is still undecided. He has sent a letter to the National Government and is awaiting a reply. Marley also responded to the report in the Japanese newspaper Shanghai Daily News that the current anti-war movement is engaged in anti-German and anti-Japanese activities, saying that the anti-war movement and the opposition to the National Socialist movement are completely two different organizations and are absolutely unrelated. Major countries now have committees to help refugees under National Socialism, and these committees have absolutely nothing to do with the Anti-War Congress. As for the activities of the anti-war movement, they are not aimed at a single country, let alone against Japan. The Japanese newspaper's statement is absolutely unfounded. Regarding the Japanese newspaper's claim that Britain is using the anti-war movement to carry out an anti-Japanese policy, Marley stated that although the anti-war movement has the support of a majority of Labor Party members, he has never received the support of the British government. Whether Britain actually has an anti-Japanese policy is also questionable.

Sun Ke and Others Go to Nanjing 112

Sun Ke, Chu Minyi, Liu Weizhi, and Ma Chaojun took the night express train to Nanjing yesterday.

Central Mint's New Coins 113

Sent to the United States for Analysis and Passed

Weight and Fineness are Within Legal Standards

Ministry of Finance Orders Commendation and Encouragement to the Mint

Since being ordered to mint new coins, the Central Mint has produced 2.26 million yuan using old molds and 9.26 million yuan using new molds by the end of August. These coins have been inspected and certified as qualified by the Review Committee and delivered to the Central Bank for issuance. To ensure public confidence, they were sent to the Philadelphia and San Francisco mints in the United States for analysis. All were within the legal standards, that is, the tolerance between the weight and fineness of each coin and the legal standard (each coin weighing 26.6971 grams, containing 88% silver and 12% copper, including 23.493448 grams of pure silver) does not exceed three thousandths. The Review Committee submitted the analysis results from the two US mints to the Ministry of Finance, which issued an order of commendation the day before yesterday, stating: "The presentation and tables are all noted. After examining the analysis results of the new coins minted by the factory and sent to the Philadelphia and San Francisco mints in the United States, all are within the legal standards. This shows that the director of the factory is effective in his supervision, and all employees are able to perform their duties. Deeply commend, in addition to filing the analysis table and publishing it in the Gazette, this order is issued."

China Production and Sales Company Hosts Banquet for Financial and Industrial Circles 117

Cao Yunxiang Speaks on the Failure of Foreign Trade

Jiang Yiping and Gu Zhuxuan Immediately Pledge to Subscribe to Shares

Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Wu Zhihao, and others, the directors and deputy directors of the preparatory office of the China National Products Production and Sales United Company, held a banquet at the Dadong Restaurant on Nanjing Road at 7:00 PM yesterday to entertain people from the financial and industrial circles of this city, as well as celebrities from various circles and the company's founders. Recently, the executive committee of the preparatory office has drafted a summary of the business plan and procedures, printed it into a book, and distributed it to the guests at the banquet, requesting as much criticism as possible in order to gather ideas widely. Those who attended the banquet included Xue Dubi, Zhu Ziqiao, Cao Yunxiang, Li Zushing, Guo Le, Wu Yunzhai, Mu Ouchu, Li Dachao, Yin Zhufu, Lu Wenshao, He Dekui, Gu Xinyi, Jiang Junyi, Wu Yunzhu, Jiang Yiping, Gu Zhuxuan, Zhao Jinqing, Wu Jingxiong, Xie Pengfei, Xu Kecheng, Cha Liangzhao, Zhu Wenqi, Tu Kaizheng, Chen Yizhou, Wu Xizhi, Tao Leqin, Gui Yanfang, Chen Jicheng, Bei Zuyi, Xue Chunsheng, Yu Qiaqing, Cai Suizhi, Yu Guozhen, Xu Chunrong, Wang Zhongcui, Xu Tingzuo, Sheng Zhiren, Zhu Xuefan, Ji Fusun, Wang Jian'e, Ren Jinping, Zhu Dechao, Wu Guangzhi, Li Wanli, Hong Jingshan, Wang Jie'an, and more than 200 others. After taking their seats in order, the chairman first reported on the preparation process of the company. The number of people who have joined as founders has reached 166, and the number of people who have joined as sponsors has reached 75. The total amount of shares that have been subscribed is 45,100 yuan. It is hoped that all founders will sign the number of shares they have subscribed for and prepare to proceed with the registration procedures. Then Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Wu Zhihao, Cao Yunxiang, Li Zushing, Wang Jie'an, Li Wanli, and others gave speeches in succession. The speeches and the number of shares subscribed on the spot are recorded below:

Wang Xiaolai's Speech 118

"The current Chinese social economy has fallen into an extremely dangerous situation. It is necessary to provide relief. To put it simply, the purpose of launching the Production and Sales United Company is to promote national products. The two words 'production and sales' may seem novel at first glance, but they are actually plain and unremarkable. I have always considered Chinese merchants to value morality. For example, when opening a store, they gather a number of people to plan the development of commerce, and they will not succeed unless they share the same goals and values. There is also the so-called 'credibility in commerce.' All merchants must be credible. The Production and Sales United Company gathers the strength of many people to seek cooperation in production and promotion, and cooperation in economy and talent. What is it if not sharing the same goals and values and conducting business with credibility? If the products of the factory are shoddy, it is a breach of faith. A breach of faith is injustice. Once credibility is lost, sales will stagnate, and failure will follow before the end of the day. The so-called Production and Sales United Company contains the meaning of sharing the same goals and values and conducting business with credibility. Therefore, the products of the factory must be excellent in order to win the trust of consumers. Production and promotion are mutually dependent, like the arms helping each other. Only then can there be hope for development. Today, all the gentlemen present are giants in the industry. I hope you will give more guidance and work together to solve the people's livelihood problems and make our China become strong and prosperous and survive in the world."

Wu Zhihao's Speech 119

"I have always considered that the governments of various countries provide detailed equipment for the encouragement of industry, such as the implementation of protective tariffs and the stipulation of export bonuses. However, our country is not only unable to implement protective tariffs due to the restrictions of various countries, but also has never seen export bonuses in laws and regulations. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and markets are declining, the government should come forward to organize production and sales matters to provide relief for the livelihoods of the majority of people and cultivate the nation's vitality. However, our government is in a time of internal and external troubles, and its finances are extremely exhausted. Therefore, it has been unable to provide sufficient assistance. This matter is now being undertaken by people from the industrial and financial circles in Shanghai. In the future, after the company is established, I hope that the government will provide assistance, such as reducing taxes and rewarding exports. These are all urgent matters to alleviate the people's livelihood and promote national products."

Cao Yunxiang's Speech 120

Mr. Cao stated that the founders of the China Products Sales United Company are all experienced businessmen. In the future, attention should be paid to sales talent. Commercial competition has many methods, but they should be directed outward, not inward. He has often seen that in the past, Chinese businesses lacked trade association organizations and were like a plate of loose sand. Not only was there no unity, but there was also jealousy among competitors. Anyone who possessed some skill or wisdom was unwilling to share it with others for mutual study and discussion. Their vision for foreign trade was shallow, only thinking about undermining each other. Without the leadership of trade associations, the results were often failures. He recalled that when he was in New York in his early years, he saw a Chinese merchant bringing tea bricks from Hankou to America for sale. The New York tea merchants were greatly alarmed and tried to prevent the sales. Later, the tea merchants contributed 100,000 yuan as a birthday gift to the Chinese merchant. The merchant, seeing profit and forgetting righteousness, suddenly obtained a large sum of money and abandoned his obligation to promote tea bricks in America. He used the money for gambling and extravagant eating. Later, this person disappeared. Also, when he was in Germany, he saw a Chinese merchant coming to Germany to sell silk. The German silk merchants agreed not to trade with him. The merchant had no choice but to auction off the silk at a low price and spent the money lavishly. The result was also a great failure. Therefore, he believes that selling goods is not an easy task, especially selling to foreign countries, because foreign merchants are often able to not be greedy for small profits and have strong solidarity, unlike Chinese merchants who only seek profit and disregard everything else.

Li Wanli's Speech 121

The China National Products Sales United Company is a product of the shift from "free economy" to controlled economy, which is now a consistent and universal trend in modern nation-building. The so-called controlled economy means production for consumers. What consumers need is what producers prepare. The entire production sector targets the entire consumer base, focusing solely on increasing production to meet consumer needs, without worrying about sales or competition among peers, in order to achieve universal sales. The aim is to ensure that all Chinese people use Chinese goods, while preventing foreign goods from being sold domestically, and then promoting Chinese goods abroad. By understanding the availability of products in various regions, and using wholesale and retail methods, the goods will be transferred to local businesses and shops for resale to the general public. In the future, each business and shop will be able to post a slogan at the entrance: "This business and shop sells only Chinese goods. Everything you buy and eat here is undoubtedly Chinese goods." This is indeed an advertisement for the production sector. The significance of the China National Products Sales United Company is so great. It is hoped that both the production and consumption sides will join together and realize it immediately. This is not only saving the country but also saving ourselves, and so on.

Eager Subscribers 122

After the speech, more than thirty or forty people participated in the initiation and sponsorship on the spot. Jiang Yiping, one of the initiators, subscribed to 10,000 yuan worth of shares. Gu Zhuxuan, Xue Qisheng, and Lu Wenshao each subscribed to 5,000 yuan worth of shares. Zhu Wenqi, Guo Le, Xie Pengfei, and Ji Fusun each subscribed to 1,000 yuan worth of shares. Jin Guanfu, Bi Zaichang, Feng Yuancheng, Xu Limin, Shen Bocun, Lou Fengshao, Dong Huaizhu, Wang Peikun, Xuan E, and Sun Guxin each subscribed to 500 yuan worth of shares. Liu Guanxiong subscribed to 300 yuan worth of shares. Shi Chunshan, Zhang Jizhi, and the Guanghua Gas Lamp Factory and Baoxing Zuo Jing Factory each subscribed to 200 yuan worth of shares. Li Wenjie subscribed to 100 yuan. On that day, a total of more than 40,000 yuan worth of shares were subscribed.

National Federation of Commerce Surveys Shanghai Industries After the War 124

Business Greatly Reduced... Many Closures

According to the Central News Agency, after the January 28th Incident following the September 18th Incident, all industries across the country suffered great losses, which have not yet been recovered. Shanghai, being located in the war zone, suffered even greater losses. Therefore, the National Federation of Commerce has compiled the situation of Shanghai's business scene before and after the war, as follows:

Financial Industry 125

The financial industry in this city has not yet fully recovered from the losses suffered in the war. In January of the 21st year, the city's cash reserve was only 73,000,000 yuan, and the silver reserve was only 61,350,000 taels. By the end of that year, the cash reserve was 242,000,000 yuan, an increase of 70,000,000 yuan compared to before the war, and the silver reserve was 13,600,000 taels, an increase of more than double. The concentration of silver in Shanghai, due to the decline of the market, made it impossible to absorb. In April of this year, the tael was abolished and the yuan was adopted. In July, the Central Mint began to mint new coins. By the end of July, the number of silver dollars in the city had increased to 275,480,000 yuan and 140,792,000 taels, an increase of more than 10% compared to last year. Although the financial industry suffered less than other industries in the January 28th Incident, the banks and native banks that were directly affected by the war and closed down include Dada Bank, Zhengda Bank, Changsheng Native Bank, Yichun Native Bank, Defeng Native Bank, Yuansheng Native Bank, Huichang Native Bank, Yuanshun Native Bank, and Yuanda Native Bank. Those that were reorganized due to the war include China Industrial Bank, Overseas Chinese Bank, Futai Native Bank, Xinyu Native Bank, Renchang Native Bank, Anyu Native Bank, Hongxiang Native Bank, Shengda Native Bank, Shenyuan Native Bank, Xinkang Native Bank, and Dingsheng Native Bank. However, new establishments also include Ningbo Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Commercial Savings Bank, Huifeng Bank, Tongyuan Commercial Savings Bank, Jia Hua Branch, Hua An Bank, Qianyi Silver Company, Siming Savings Society, Overseas Chinese Trust Company, and Shengchang Native Bank.

Industry and Commerce 126

(1) Cotton Spinning Industry: The Shanghai factory's yarn production mainly relied on sales in North China. Since the fall of the Northeast, the sales of Chinese yarn factories have been declining daily, leading to overproduction. Some have implemented a system of reduced working hours, while others have requested assistance. The situation is particularly bleak, while Japanese yarn factories have been able to implement dumping. Therefore, many Chinese factories have closed down or reduced their scale. (2) Cotton Weaving Industry: During the Shanghai war, about sixteen or seventeen Chinese cotton weaving factories were destroyed. The most prosperous period for cotton cloth and foreign goods stores saw over a thousand in the city. After this blow, one-third have closed down in the past year, leaving only about six hundred. The native cloth industry has also seen a significant decrease in business due to the loss of the Northeast. Other small

cloth manufacturers are also barely surviving. (2) Silk Industry: There were originally 112 silk factories in the city, with 25,300 looms. Production almost completely ceased during the Shanghai Incident. About a dozen were destroyed by artillery fire. By June of last year, only 31 had resumed production. In November, with government assistance, 65 had resumed production. Two-fifths have not yet resumed production. (4) Flour Industry: The total production capacity of all flour mills in Shanghai can reach 33 million bags per year at its peak. After the war, some produced less than 10 million bags. Wheat and other grains were also affected by the situation, with 60-70% relying on foreign wheat. (5) Cigarette Industry: The Shanghai cigarette factories reached over 180 at their peak. Now only about sixty remain. Other industries are also declining year by year.

Page 13

Japan Plans to Monopolize Our Textile Market 127

Preparing to Improve Factories in China

According to the Central News Agency, Japanese merchants have established more than 40 yarn factories in Shanghai and other ports in China, with more than 1.7 million spindles and more than 200,000 thread spindles, producing approximately 800,000 bales of yarn and more than 10 million bolts of cloth annually. This has a significant impact on domestic yarn and cloth manufacturers. However, due to the global recession and weak purchasing power of the people, the general business situation is bleak. It is now heard that Japanese merchants, in order to win the commercial war, have decided to improve their machinery and reduce costs. Therefore, there is a comprehensive plan to uniformly convert all factories in China to new-style textile machines, with each 400 spindles requiring only one person to manage. Not only is the weaving precise, but the cost is also low, with the aim of monopolizing the Chinese textile market.

Importation of Dutch Goods Requires Presentation of a Certificate of Origin 128

According to the Great American Evening News, this port recently received an official report that the Dutch Minister of Economic Affairs and Labor has ordered that all imports of woolen fabrics, wool-silk fabrics, wool-cotton fabrics, coats, porcelain, pottery, tiles, socks, dyed prints, and embroidered cotton cloth shoes and zinc foil must be presented with a certificate of origin.

It is recorded in the file. Regarding the level of public friendship, etc., it is hereby approved. The fifth standing committee meeting decided to send letters to the district sub-associations to inform the members to investigate and handle it as a whole."

Japanese Navy Stationed in China Changes the September 18th Drill 132

Mobile Police Officers Continue to Come to China

More than 20 warships belonging to the Japanese Navy's Third Fleet in Shanghai and the First Expeditionary Force in the Yangtze River were originally scheduled to hold a large exercise outside Wusong on the 15th. Therefore, the 27 fleet ships patrolling outside have returned to Shanghai yesterday, and the Japanese warships in the Yangtze River were originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai today to gather. However, because September 18th is the date of the Japanese army's invasion of Shenyang, the Japanese naval authorities in Shanghai have decided to change the date of the Shanghai Third Fleet exercise to the 18th of this month in order to show their triumph. The Japanese warships in the Yangtze River will also postpone their arrival in Shanghai by a few days. As for the review of the stationed Shanghai Marine Corps, it has already been held in the branch. It is known that 450 members of the naval regiment brought by the Chizhi warship have been added to the Shanghai Marine Corps, and the 300 members who should be transferred back have left Shanghai for Japan. As for the period after the January 28th Incident, the Japanese police authorities specially trained a kind of mobile police. The method is to transfer Japanese police officers of all levels, from middle to lower, to China in batches every month, about 30 to 40 people, to conduct on-the-spot investigations of the Chinese situation, moving and rotating in succession. On the one hand, they are continuously sent from Japan, and on the other hand, the police officers stationed in China whose terms have expired are also transferred back to their home country in succession. If this is done, in a year or two, all Japanese police officers will be completely transformed into those who are deeply aware of the Chinese situation. This mobile police force has never stopped since the January 28th Incident, and continues to be dispatched and transferred. This is also continuously happening.

Silk Factory Labor Unrest Has Many Twists and Turns 133

Chuxin Strikes Again Due to the Change to a New Scale

The Dayangqiao Area Has Been Persuaded to Resume Work

The labor unrest in the silk factories has been delayed and unresolved, leading to many twists and turns. The striking workers in the Xinzha District harassed the Dayangqiao area north of the railway the day before yesterday, causing the Fengtai and other twelve factories in the area to also be affected by the strike. With the persuasion of the Fifty Trade Union, all resumed work yesterday. Only Chuxin and Yuanfeng in the Xinzha District started work yesterday, but unexpectedly, Chuxin struck again in the afternoon due to the change to a new scale. The details are as follows:

Swarming Harassment 134

At 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, about four to five hundred striking workers from the factories in the Xinzha District gathered and swarmed to harass the Dayangqiao area, damaging a lot of Fengtai's bamboo fences, causing the factory workers to lose interest in working and declare a strike. The strike spread to Fuchang, Yutai, Gongda, Tiansheng, Hongxi, Yingji, Hengcang, Xinglun, Yufeng, and other eleven silk factories at the same time.

Persuading to Start Work 135

At 4:00 a.m. this morning, the Sixth District Silk Industry Trade Union specially sent all the directors and supervisors, including Yang Gengti and Yuan Yunlong, as well as staff members Fei Guojie, etc., to the Dayangqiao Liutiaoying and Tanziwan to persuade the factories to blow their horns and start work. All the workers were also persuaded by the trade union to resume work. At the same time, in order to prevent the Xinzha workers from harassing them again, people were stationed on the main roads to dissuade them. Fortunately, no new twists and turns occurred.

Chuxin Changes Scale 136

Chuxin on Chang'an Road and Yuanfeng on Hengfeng Road in the Xinzha District resumed work yesterday because they were selling forward silk for settlement. The remaining twenty-one factories, such as Maofeng and Wuxing, did not start work because they were afraid of new twists and turns. Unexpectedly, yesterday, the Chuxin side changed the original line scale to a liang scale (the liang scale is 75% of the line scale) and did not pay the weekly bonus for last week. The factory workers believed that this move by the management violated the decisions made by the Social Bureau on July 8th and September 7th and reimplemented the new system, and they rose up in opposition. Therefore, after the meal break, they declared a strike. The trade union reported the situation and went to investigate. The management had already destroyed the scale. Fortunately, with the protection of the police, Yuanfeng was not affected.

Wages Remain the Same 137

The Sixth District Silk Industry Trade Union, fearing that the workers would misunderstand again, specially wrote a wage chart this morning and posted it on the gates of each factory to reassure the workers to work. The original text reads: "The wages of female workers in the silk factories in this district will remain the same. The first-class wage is 50 cents, the weekly bonus is 20 cents, and the bonus for hard work is 20 cents. It is hoped that everyone will continue to work with peace of mind and no longer misunderstand."

Notifying All Factories 138

The Sixth District Silk Industry Council, Notice No. 66, for the purpose of notification, the management suddenly changed to a production system, causing fierce opposition from the female workers,

and causing labor unrest. The association has already submitted a request to the Social Bureau to preside over the investigation, and the management has long been ordered not to implement it. However, the female workers have shallow knowledge and are easily incited by others, and have repeatedly failed to resume work, causing direct losses to the factory and indirectly affecting the livelihoods of the workers. Now, in order to make it easier for the female workers to understand, the staff of each factory are requested to earnestly explain to the female workers under their management, work with peace of mind, and no longer listen to rumors. They are also requested to pay attention to the actions of the female workers. If there are reactionary elements lurking in the female worker ranks, taking the opportunity to incite and incite, please report or detain them to the association, and a considerable reward will be given as an encouragement. This is hereby notified, and it is hoped that everyone will abide by it. September 12th, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Disaster Relief News from Lu and Yu 139

Heze Begs for Relief　　Representatives of the Shandong Heze County Flood Relief Association, Ran Fanrui, Ge Xiangyi, Guo Junqing, etc., sent a letter to the Yellow River Flood Relief Association yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, this time, the Yellow River breached in the provinces of Ji and Yu, and western Shandong was flooded. The magnitude of the flood is unprecedented, especially in Heze, which suffered the most severe damage. The water depth in the plains is four to five feet to more than one zhang. Four-fifths of the county's 1,800 villages were submerged. The new grain has not been harvested, and the old grain has been washed away by the water. According to statistics, the total loss in the county is more than 30 million yuan. There are more than 300,000 disaster victims in the county, without food, clothing, or shelter. At present, the disaster victims need food the most, followed by clothing, and then shelter. Transportation in Heze is inconvenient, and it is quite difficult to transport relief supplies purchased from afar. It has been found that the harvest in neighboring areas that have not been flooded is not very bad. It is best to purchase goods nearby or release cash to avoid the labor of transportation. The price of grain is one corner of a silver dollar, which can buy two catties of millet. The route to Heze is: first, from Ji to the west, travel more than 20 miles by land to Heshangkou, cross the Zhushui River to Xuzhuang, and then hire a rickshaw to reach the county seat via Zhifang, Dayi Ji, Shanhai, Xinji, and other villages. Second, transfer from Xuzhou to the Longhai Road to Liuhe Station, and then go through Caoxian County and Dingtao County to the county seat. This is a joint association of Shanghai charitable organizations raising emergency relief for the Yellow River flood, with a map of the disaster area attached."

Liu Zhi's Thank You Telegram 140

The Yellow River Flood Relief Association received a reply telegram from Liu Zhi, Chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, yesterday, stating: "The Shanghai Charitable Organizations' Yellow River Flood Relief Joint Association, Committee Member Xu, Brother Junren, transfer to Deputy Committee Member Wang Xunjian, respectfully received the good telegram. The Yellow River flood is deeply appreciated for raising funds for emergency relief. In addition to ordering the subordinates to properly protect and assist as requested, a special telegram is sent to welcome you and express gratitude. Respectfully request that all charitable organizations be notified, Liu Zhi, Chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, sincerely."

Urging Chen Yi and Zou Lin to Come to Shanghai Early 141

Because it is necessary to investigate the accounts and vouchers of the donations handled by the various national salvation donation organizations in this city, a Committee for Investigating National Salvation Donations has been organized to start the investigation. The Executive Yuan, because the matter is

serious, the government cannot ignore it and has appointed Vice Minister of Military and Political Affairs Chen Yi and Vice Minister of Finance Zou Lin as special investigators to come to Shanghai for thorough investigation. Upon hearing the news, the Committee for Investigating National Salvation Donations in various circles sent a special express mail telegram to the two, asking them to come to Shanghai as soon as possible so that the investigation could be completed as soon as possible. The original telegram is as follows: "Public Xia Yulin, Minister Xunjian, the various national salvation donation organizations in Shanghai are rumored to have embezzled donations, and all citizens are indignant and full of indignation. Our association has previously telegraphed the central government to send personnel for thorough investigation to clarify the truth and show great credibility. Now, seeing in the newspaper that the Executive Yuan has appointed you as special investigators, we are extremely happy. However, this matter has occurred for nearly two months, and the impact on the future of anti-Japanese donations is not small. On behalf of all citizens, we urge you to come to Shanghai as soon as possible to instruct our association to assist in the investigation and complete the mission together. We are extremely eager. The Shanghai Committee for Investigating National Salvation Donations sincerely."

Aviation Association Announces Recruitment Results of Each Team 143

Wang Yansong Recruits

Municipal Public Works Bureau Water Supply Design 145

Establish a Water Supply Office West of Xujiahui

Gradually Promote to Zhenru and Wusong

Regarding the Municipal Public Works Bureau's preparations for the Pudong Waterworks, Section Chief Zhu of the Bureau's Second Section told a Central News Agency reporter yesterday that the Bureau had drafted a plan in 1930, stipulating an expenditure of 600,000 yuan, and after being approved by the municipal meeting in 1931, it purchased two plots of land in Taoyuan Village, Lannidu, Pudong, for the construction of factory buildings and reservoirs. When it was in progress, the January 28th Incident happened, and it was suspended indefinitely. Now, although the Municipal Public Works Bureau is eager to continue the project, it is difficult to realize it for a while because the municipal treasury is more difficult than before. Zhu also said that in order to facilitate the water use of citizens in the section west of Xujiahui, where there is no tap water equipment, the Public Works Bureau has borrowed 15,000 yuan from the Municipal Bank to establish a water supply office for citizens to purchase. Water can be supplied in two weeks. In the future, depending on the financial resources, it will be extended to Zhenru, Wusong, and other districts, as well as Pudong, so that the Pudong water supply problem can be solved.

Appeal Regarding the Typhoon Disaster in Chuansha 148

On the second of this month, a hurricane passed through Shanghai, causing incalculable losses to crops in Chuansha and Nanhui in Pudong, especially in Hengsha, Gaodunsha, Yuanyuansha, and other areas under the jurisdiction of Chuansha, which suffered the most severe damage. When the storm surge arrived, houses were destroyed and people and animals were drowned. Local officials and gentry, after receiving the report, went by boat to survey the damage and saw disaster victims everywhere, their cries shaking the fields. Not only is the autumn harvest hopeless, but even

the spring plowing next year will have no seeds. On the same day, money and rice were distributed, and coffins were transported to collect corpses, but it was a drop in the bucket and did not solve the problem. Legislative Yuan Compiles and Publishes a Compilation of Constitutions of Various Countries 150

All our citizens yearn for the promulgation of the Constitution. Since Mr. Sun Zhesheng became the head of the Legislative Yuan, he has devoted all his efforts to this. Now, the draft of the Constitution has been prepared, and the ambassadors of various countries stationed in China have been entrusted to collect the current Constitutions of their respective governments. Constitutions of more than forty countries, such as Britain, Russia, Germany, Austria, the United States, and France, have been collected. Special renowned Chinese and foreign scholars have been hired to compile them into a book entitled "Compilation of Constitutions of Various Countries," for reference in the drafting of the Constitution. It is also a must-read book for the people of our country during the constitutional period. The book has been exquisitely printed and published by the Shanghai Sima Road Wangping Street Hanwen Zhengkai Printing House with movable type in regular script. The entire book has more than 700 pages, and is bound in a gold-stamped cloth cover, priced at six yuan and eight jiao. In order to assist in constitutional government, the bureau has set a special price for two months, with each book costing only four yuan. It is reported that the Legislative Yuan has issued an order to all provincial governments to purchase the book uniformly.

=The government authorities are considering it=

=Rumors that it will be abandoned are not true=

In short, in order to develop Sino-Russian trade, our country will establish a special bureau for trade with Russia, or use other methods to seek relief. The government authorities are currently considering it. I have not heard anything yet. Baoshan Farmers' Amateur Recreational Association 152

Jifubridge in Baoshan County is located at the intersection of the second, third, fourth, and fifth districts of the county. Transportation has always been inconvenient and the people's knowledge is rudimentary. Since the Farmers' Education Center initiated the organization of rural improvement districts, some construction has been done for local undertakings and unnecessary consumption has also gradually decreased. For example, there has not been a single lawsuit in July and August. However, according to rural customs, there are often flower drum performances and other events during the autumn harvest, which are of great importance to local customs. Now, in order to eliminate bad habits and promote proper entertainment, village leaders Zong Baozhu, Shi Shangzhen, Zong Baozhong, etc., have been holding a farmers' amateur recreational association at the North Zong residence for two days starting yesterday. The programs include national martial arts, silk and bamboo music, speeches, and improved Shanghai opera, etc. They also invited Ji Zhonghe, director of the Farmers' Education Center, to give a speech, the main points of which were: (1) Improving entertainment and having fun in a timely manner are indispensable to life, but happiness comes from suffering, and we should think of suffering when we are happy, and not forget suffering; (2) Increasing knowledge and skills, the survey shows that only 30% of the people in this area are literate, so more people should attend public schools; (3) Strengthening physical fitness, we should practice national martial arts, which can not only strengthen the body, but at least defend ourselves; (4) Reducing consumption, we should quit bad habits such as smoking opium and gambling; (5) Increasing production, we should pay attention to improving agricultural planting, and give more instructions on improving cotton planting methods. The listeners were moved. It is said that there were more than 6,000 people present, which is a good opportunity for education.

Saving the Country with Science, Chinese Establish a Domestic Calcium Carbide Factory 155

Important raw material in industry

Performance better than imported products

Shanghai business giants Kui Yanfang, Yu Zuoting, Jin Tingsun, Shi Zhikun, Xue Runsheng, etc., felt that domestic industry was becoming increasingly developed, but the raw materials were still dependent on imports, and the annual leakage was huge. They initiated the establishment of the China Calcium Carbide Factory. Calcium carbide occupies an important position in industry, such as welding steel, iron, copper, and machinery parts, manufacturing acetic acid, rayon, air fertilizer, airplane paint, military explosives, and smokeless gunpowder. All are necessary raw materials. Therefore, various countries also regard it as a necessary commodity for national defense. Recently, the factory's engineer and electrochemist, Mr. Shi Yunchang, equipped electrical equipment and carefully tested it, achieving remarkable results. At 4:00 PM yesterday, a public test was held on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association. Guests from all walks of life arrived one after another. Mr. Shi arranged equipment to trial-produce a small amount of calcium carbide, and it was completely successful after more than an hour. The domestically produced calcium carbide and the imported calcium carbide on the market were tested with the same amount. For the calcium carbide gas, each gram of imported calcium carbide can produce 290 cc of gas, while the domestically produced calcium carbide can produce 450 cc of gas. The quality is more beautiful compared to imported products. All visitors admired it. The establishment of the factory in the future will also be a boon for the future of national industry and national defense.
