Yang Xuezhong Sentenced for Enticing a Young Girl 159

Ji Mingquan, from Xuzhou, lives in Ronghua Lane on Robison Road in West Shanghai, and his daughter Ji Dadu, who is only 15 years old, is taken care of by Ji Sheng, a Chinese constable at No. 1657, Public Concession. Ji returned to his hometown in early summer due to business. Unexpectedly, at about 7:00 PM on June 27, the girl was taken away by her uncle, Yang Xuezhong, and entrusted to friends Feng Zhaoming, Lin Chunfa, Wu Yaoting, and Gao Fengshi, etc., to marry Zhou Jingquan, an apprentice of Du Wanshun, as his wife. Du Wanshun paid 130 yuan in betrothal money. Subsequently, on August 7, Yang, the Chinese constable at No. 1657, discovered that the girl had been taken away by her uncle, Yang Xuezhong, and that her father, Ji Mingquan, had not given him custody rights. Believing that there was an act of enticement, he reported it to the Putuo Road Police Station and arrested all the criminals. He filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai First Special District Local Court in accordance with Article 257, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, which prohibits crimes against marriage and family, and Article 240, Paragraph 2, which prohibits crimes against morality. Judge Liu presided over the interrogation and deemed it necessary to summon the girl's father, Ji Mingquan, to court to testify. After several postponements, on the morning of the 9th of this month, Judge Wu Ting took the seat in the Eighth Tribunal to conduct a new trial. The defendants Du Wanshun and Zhou Jingquan elected lawyers Long Wenhuan, etc., as joint defenders and summoned witnesses for interrogation and postponement. Yesterday (the 11th), the trial continued. Lawyers Long Wenhuan, the defense lawyers for Du and Zhou, gave a torrential eloquent argument, believing that except for the defendant Yang Xuezhong, the other defendants were unaware of the situation and could not establish a criminal act, requesting that they be declared innocent. All the defendants denied that they had committed seduction. Judge Wu reviewed the confessions and announced that the court would postpone the trial and appoint a defense attorney for further interrogation. The defendants were returned to custody.

The judge announced the verdict in court. The defendant Yang Xuezhong was sentenced to three years of imprisonment for the crime of enticing a woman under the age of 20 to leave the person with parental rights. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be offset by two days for one day of imprisonment. All other defendants were found not guilty. After hearing the verdict, Lawyer Gong immediately asked the court to release the defendants who were found not guilty in court, and the court approved.

Yu euphemistically dissuaded her because she was pregnant, but she became angry, secretly took her jewelry, and quietly returned to her mother's home, never to return, and filed a lawsuit for no reason, intentionally making unreasonable demands, and demanding a huge amount of alimony from him to settle the matter, which was extremely cunning. If seduction is discussed, Xiuzhen should be responsible for the crime, which has nothing to do with Yu, because he was forced by Xiuzhen at the time, and threatened to commit suicide. Please dismiss the original lawsuit, so that the broken mirror can be reunited. Yesterday, Chief Judge Feng Shide of the First Special Court summoned both parties for interrogation. Betel Nut Brand Cigarette Prize Coupons 172

Another First Prize Discovered

=Zhu Qichang Also Has Prize Coupon No. 226622=

=Accusing Hua Dong Tobacco Company Manager Li of Fraud=

The China Hua Dong Tobacco Company, in order to promote Betel Nut Brand cigarettes, issued a prize coupon for sales promotion, divided into two series, totaling

one million numbers. There were two first prizes, each worth five thousand yuan. The prize drawing dates and numbers were based on the standards of the Aviation Prize Coupons. On July 31st, the winning number for the first prize of the aviation lottery was 226622. The winner was Zhu Wenjiang, a Chinese constable with badge number 3173 from the General Patrol Room, who claimed his prize money from the company on August 5th. Later, Li Dongtao claimed that he also had a prize coupon with the same number, but the Hua Dong Company refused to pay. He sued in the First Special Court, and as a result, the manager of the Hua Dong Tobacco Company,

Li Xuedong, was declared innocent. All these details were reported in this newspaper. Recently,

Zhu Qichang from Anhui Province stated that he also held a Betel Nut Brand prize coupon with the number 226622. He had requested payment from the Hua Dong Tobacco Company but was unsuccessful. Therefore, he hired lawyer Tang Youwei to file a fraud lawsuit in the First Special Court against Li Xuedong, the manager of Hua Dong, and Li Runsheng, the assistant manager. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng presided over the hearing in the Fifth Criminal Court. Both defendants, accompanied by their legal representative, lawyer Chen Zhongyin, appeared in court to handle the case. Zhu Qichang was absent and was represented by lawyer Tang, who outlined the key points of the prosecution, stating that in July, Zhu exchanged five Betel Nut Brand hard-pack cigarette boxes for a prize coupon from the Hua Dong Tobacco Company. When the prize was drawn on July 31st, Zhu's number matched the first prize, and he was overjoyed. On August 1st, he inquired about the procedure for claiming the prize at the company but was told that the prize money had already been claimed and that he was too late. Zhu found this matter quite strange and entrusted his lawyer to negotiate on his behalf, but to no avail. Hence the lawsuit. However, according to newspaper reports, the prize money was claimed on August 5th, while Zhu Qichang inquired at the company on August 1st. At that time, the company staff claimed that the prize money had already been claimed, which raises suspicions. Furthermore, why are there so many first prize winners? This should be investigated. A civil suit is also attached, seeking compensation of five thousand yuan. Li Runsheng testified that he was only in charge of the company's financial transactions and had no knowledge of the prize coupon matters. Li Xuedong stated that the prize coupons were printed by Da Xing Printing Factory, and Xie Long Tobacco Company was the general manager. Due to a temporary oversight by the printing factory, some coupons were mistakenly printed with duplicate numbers, resulting in blank coupons being issued rashly. However, the details of this matter can be proven by someone from the printing factory, and the previous case had already testified in court. Judge Huang reviewed the testimony and adjourned the case for further hearing. Both defendants withdrew.

Dancer Zhang Aina Loses Her Virginity to a College Student 173

=Passionate Love Precedes Bitter Breakup=

=Her Mother Now Files a Lawsuit=

Zhang Wangshi, a 45-year-old woman from Zhujing Town, Jinshan County, Songjiang, has a daughter named Zhang Aina, who is 18 years old. With a charming appearance, she entered the Lafayette dance hall as a dancer due to her family's poverty, living a life of embraces and using her earnings to support her elderly mother, relying on each other to survive. A certain university student named Xu Jiaqing, 22 years old from Guangdong, residing at No. 39 Ruihua Lane, Lafayette Road, in a two-story building, is the son of an official family and has a considerable amount of wealth. Jiaqing is a dissolute young

man, a handsome youth who likes to indulge in entertainment. He often visits the Lafayette dance hall with two or three friends. He was immediately captivated by Aina's beautiful face, considering her a celestial being. He pursued her relentlessly, seducing her with sweet words. On April 28th of this year, she was lured to the Grand Shanghai Hotel. Xu falsely claimed to the girl that he was not yet married, discussed marriage with her, and even wrote a statement promising that he would never be unfaithful, otherwise he would be willing to compensate for all losses. At the time, Aina was young and inexperienced, believing Jiaqing's solemn oath to be true. She fell into his trap and allowed him to rape her. From then on, her purity was stained, and she could never wash away the shame. Aina still thought that since there was a marriage agreement, they would be husband and wife in the future, so she allowed him to continue to sexually assault her. Later, Aina learned that Xu Jiaqing was already married. When she confronted him, Xu not only showed no sign of comfort but even spoke rudely and stopped visiting her altogether. Aina, helpless, told her mother, Zhang Wangshi, about the situation. Zhang Wangshi, as her legal guardian, hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation in the Second Special District Court, accusing Xu of abduction and also filing a civil lawsuit to recover losses. The court accepted the case and summoned both parties the other day, scheduling a hearing for this afternoon.

Notice from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to All 175

All Industry Associations Should Re-elect as Soon as Possible

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to all industry associations yesterday, urging them to re-elect as soon as possible. The notice is recorded as follows: Respectfully, on the eleventh of this month, we received instruction No. 15047 from the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, stating that after investigation, it was found that there are a total of one hundred and sixty or so industry associations in this city

that have been reorganized and established in accordance with the current laws and regulations. It has now been more than three years, and the terms of office of the staff have long expired. Many of them have been re-elected in accordance with the law, but there are also many that have not been re-elected. We hereby order that your association comply and promptly inform the relevant industry associations that have not been re-elected to convene a meeting of member representatives on a regular basis and hold re-elections in accordance with the law, which is important, and so on. Upon receiving this, we inquired about the staff of the industry associations. According to the articles of association, their

terms of office are set at four years, and half of them should be re-elected every two years and cannot be re-elected. The first re-election is determined by drawing lots, but when the number of committee members is odd, the number of those retained may be one more than those re-elected. All have clear regulations. If the association has been established for more than two years and has not held a re-election, it is not in compliance with the law and should convene a general meeting as soon as possible to carry out the re-election in order to comply with the regulations. The corresponding recording order is hereby relayed, hoping that your association will take note of it.

Three Buddhist Organizations Welcomed European Buddhists' Delegation Yesterday 176

Hundreds of Chinese and Foreign Guests Attended

The Forewarning of Eastern Culture Spreading to Europe

A group of thirteen Buddhists from France, Germany, Italy, Belgium, and other countries, including Viro Abbate, Sitibo Buddha, Ubala, Anukung Bajia, Patilla Fa, Ufaba, Sashipu, Dalu Bi, etc., arrived in Shanghai on July 25th. They resided in Jue Lu on Da Xi Road, studying Chinese Buddhism. The Chinese Buddhist Association, Shanghai Buddhist Association, Buddhist Pure Land Society, and other three organizations, recognized that Viro's visit to China was a sign of friendly religious practitioners coming to China to study Buddhism, a forewarning of Eastern culture spreading to Europe. Therefore, they held a welcome meeting at Jue Garden on Hede Road yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM and invited Chinese and foreign people to attend, which was very grand for a time. The details obtained are recorded below.

Yellow River Flood Relief Entertainment 177

Inviting the Midget to Set Up a Ring

丨Today is the Last Day丨

The Shanghai Yellow River Flood Relief Entertainment Fair is being held at the Great World. It is only open today and will not be extended. In order to encourage people from all walks of life to help the disaster victims and arouse the interest of tourists, in addition to the original

wonderful dramas and the performances by all the martial arts experts in the National Martial Arts Hall, Luo from Wenzhou (nicknamed "Midget") was specially invited to set up a ring and use the plum blossom pile martial arts for sparring. His skills are amazing. It is said that all the actors are volunteering. Visitors can enjoy themselves and also save the starving and drowning victims, which is a win-win situation.

Attendees 178

In addition to Zhao Kong and the thirteen Buddhists from France, Germany, Italy, and Belgium, Viro, etc., the attendees were Zhu Qinglan, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Liande, Jian Yujie, Huang Hanzhi, Guan Jiongzhi, Zhao Yunshao, Li Jingwei, Huang Yichang, Liang Muwen, Zhang Yuanpei, Lu Si'an, De Hao, Mingdao, Hongsan, and foreign guests such as Dr. Fuchs from Germany, Mrs.乔洛, Ms.沙罗门, Mrs.罗路姆非而违, Mrs.克东,韦旱脱, Mrs.发立士,克罗耳, and representatives from all walks of life, totaling several hundred people.

Welcome Address 179

Mingdao Shi and Guan Jiongzhi were publicly elected as chairpersons, and Zhao Puzhu and Wang Junhe were the recorders. The ceremony was held according to the regulations, and everyone stood in silence. After the chanting of the name of Sakyamuni Buddha and the Mi Fo verse, Mingdao Shi first delivered the welcome address, which was translated into English by Guan Jiongzhi and recorded by a reporter from Heping News Agency.

Page 16

The welcome address is as follows: Today, the Chinese Buddhist Association, the Shanghai Buddhist Association, and the Buddhist Pure Land Society have prepared simple refreshments and invited everyone to come together, and we are deeply honored. It is extremely rare for Europeans to come to China to study, especially to study Buddhism and be willing to be ordained as monks. You can be considered the first group to understand and accept Chinese culture. This is the most gratifying thing in the world. The fundamental essence of Buddhism is to teach people to eliminate delusions. Those who study Buddhism must control and guard their six senses: eyes, ears, nose, tongue, body, and mind, preventing them from seeking outwards. They must let go of all the worldly burdens in order to gain the true benefits of Buddhism, because Buddhism is definitely not obtained from the outside. You have come from Europe to this place, abandoning all material enjoyments and worldly affections, not hesitating to travel tens of thousands of miles with hardship, and not hesitating to overcome various difficulties in living, eating, and speaking, dedicating yourselves to studying inner civilization and the true path. This shows that you are truly able to eliminate delusions and let go of external ties. This is the true practice of Buddhism and deserves our joy and praise. We hope that each of you will take on the task of Sakyamuni Buddha and become meritorious officials in spreading Buddhism to all sentient beings. We wish you all success.

Zhao Kong's Speech 180

Next, Zhao Kong gave a speech entitled "The Path of the Buddha," which was translated into Chinese by a reporter from Heping News Agency. It briefly stated that the Buddha is omniscient and omnipotent. If people can practice according to the Buddhist Dharma, they can also reach the position of omniscience and omnipotence. The purpose of Buddhism is not to make people become scholars, nor is it to instill many books and their formulas and laws into people's minds through such pseudo-education. In fact, true knowledge cannot be found in books. The purpose of the Buddha is to seek the fundamental knowledge and methods for people to escape from this world of suffering, so that they can enter the true gate of Nirvana. The methods are briefly described as follows: (1) Strictly observe the precepts, that is, do not kill, do not steal, do not commit adultery, do not lie, do not drink alcohol, and other precepts. (2) Guard the six senses, that is, the eyes do not pursue color, the ears do not pursue sound, the nose does not pursue fragrance, the tongue does not pursue taste, the body does not pursue touch, and the mind does not pursue the Dharma. (3) Be mindful of walking when walking, staying when staying, sitting when sitting, and lying down when lying down. (4) According to the removal of the five aggregates, remove greed, remove hatred, remove sleepiness, remove distraction,

remove doubt. (5) Practice the four foundations of mindfulness, observing the body as impure, observing sensation as suffering, observing the mind as impermanent, and observing non-self. (6) Practice the four right efforts, eliminate the evil that has already arisen, prevent the evil that has not yet arisen, generate the good that has not yet arisen, and increase the good that has already arisen. At this point, the Dharma master recounted the wonders of the four dhyanas and eight samadhis and the six supernatural powers, quoting the scriptures and being extremely profound. Those who heard it were all delighted and praised him.

Public Acknowledgment and Gratitude 181

After Zhao Kong's speech, Stan Kai, a German disciple representing Master Zhao Kong, gave a thank-you speech. After following Master Zhao Kong to Huashan, we were warmly welcomed by everyone and are extremely grateful. The Chinese people have been studying Buddhism since before the Age of Teachings and know the path to true knowledge. Seeing their gentle, compassionate, and peaceful virtues, we know that they have been deeply influenced by Buddhism. This is our first time coming to China, and we have seen this kind of atmosphere everywhere in China. We are very fortunate to be able to study Buddhism together with the Chinese people. Next, Xue Fu, representing the French disciples, gave a speech. When we arrived in China on July 25th, everyone came to the pier to welcome us and sent us to Jue Lu. I immediately felt everyone's kindness. We followed our teacher to China because we wanted to leave the world and become monks and nuns in the Buddhist country. You are our fellow brothers and sisters, and we hope that you will work with us to create blessings for China and the world. Then, the meeting adjourned.

Woman Convicted for Passing Counterfeit Coins 183

Sentenced to Three Years in Prison

Tao Wu, a woman from Nanyang, recently colluded with a fellow villager, Mr. Jia, in the Yangshupu Yinxianggang Dongzhakou area, specializing in using counterfeit Yuan head silver dollars to deceive small vendors for profit. At around 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, Wang Penghao from Taizhou set up a bamboo utensil stall in the area. The woman asked Jia to buy a bundle of chopsticks, priced at fifteen copper yuan.

She also bought two catties of taro from Ma Jinchun and others from Pudong, priced at twenty-four copper yuan. They first each gave a genuine silver dollar, and the two small vendors took them to a nearby cigarette and paper shop to have them checked before putting them in their pockets to get change. The woman then tried to switch the coins, saying that the silver dollars all had hard prints and could not be mistaken, deliberately taking them back to

inspect them, taking advantage of the opportunity to replace them with counterfeit coins. Her technique was nimble, and the two vendors were unaware that they had suddenly become counterfeit money. However, Zhu Guixian and Zhu Xiansheng, who were nearby, saw it and told the horse vendor to pay attention to the silver dollar. Ma checked his pocket again and found that it was indeed different from the previous silver dollar. He ran to the cigarette and paper shop to have it checked and confirmed that it was a counterfeit coin. He immediately grabbed the woman and argued with her. At this time, Jia had already fled without a trace. Hua Tan Liu Changgen arrived, inquired about the situation, and arrested the woman. Small vendor Wang Penghao also checked the coin he had received for the chopsticks and found that it was also made of copper. He informed Detective Liu, and they took the woman to the Yangshupu Police Station. The police chief ordered female patrol officer Gu Zhang to search the woman, and they found three more counterfeit coins of the same type in her left sock. She was sent to a women's detention center. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin detailed the situation, stating that the defendant had claimed at the police station that the copper coins had been obtained from selling half a dan of rice in Shanghai, which was completely false. It was found that she had committed the same crime eleven years ago and had been dealt with for a month. He presented the counterfeit coins and requested that she be punished. Small vendors Ma Jinchun and Wang Penghao, and witnesses Zhu Guixian and Zhu Xiansheng, gave their statements. When questioned, the defendant stammered and begged for forgiveness. Judge Wu Zihan sentenced Tao Wu to three years in prison, and the counterfeit coins were confiscated and destroyed.

Strange Fire Report in Caishi Street 187

Where Does the Red Light Come From?

Is Someone Spreading Rumors?

The Zhang Guowei Hospital and the house where the carpenter monk lives on Caishi Street (behind the Great World) in the French Concession are neighbors. At 2:30 AM yesterday (the twelfth), the roof of the building was glowing red. The neighbors thought it was a fire. In a short time, fire trucks arrived at the area around the area. Firefighters searched the street near where the fire was suspected to be but the houses had no fire. There were five or six fire trucks that arrived. After the fire trucks checked and found that there were no fires, they drove back. After the incident, the police learned of it and sent detectives to check the three-story building of the carpenter monk's house. There were no signs of fire. They then checked the three-story building of Dr. Zhang Guowei's place, and there was no fire either. The detectives returned to the police station to report. According to the neighbors, there were many people who saw the fire on the roof. However, there is a fox spirit hall on the third floor of the building. Some say that the fox spirit is causing trouble, but this is not known. Those who witnessed the red light on the roof were amazed and could not stop talking about it.

With ten points as passing, those with fifty points or more will be awarded a prize certificate, and those with one hundred points or more will be awarded a silver shield.

The Fourth Issue of "Current Affairs Compilation" by the Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center is Published 192

The fourth issue of "Current Affairs Compilation," compiled and translated by the Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center, has been published. The content of this issue is rich, totaling more than 60,000 words. In terms of manuscripts, apart from the article "The World Trade That Is Being Eliminated," which is a continuation, the other articles, "The Origin of Economic Nationalism," "France's Oil Policy," "Prospects for the International Oil and Food War," "British Overseas Investment," and "Phenomena in the Development of Economic Panic," analyze the current state of economic competition among various countries in the world in an extremely thorough manner, especially clarifying the oil hegemony war among Britain, the United States, France, and the Soviet Union. In addition, there is also the article "Why Are There Progressive Schools?" which is a recent work by Dr. Dewey, a prominent figure in the American education community. This article explains and criticizes the weaknesses of modern education and the new trends in future education, which is indeed an important issue that people in our country today should pay attention to. The general sales agent for this publication is the Zuozhe Bookstore on Fourth Malu in this city. The retail price is one dime per copy, and the annual subscription is 3.20 yuan.

Spring and Autumn

Thieves 203

— Bai He

"Thief" and "robber" are naturally not "law-abiding citizens," but there are still some differences in status. In China, it seems that the status of a thief is much higher. Being a thief seems to be worthy of praise. For example, Mr. Tang Jieyuan Bo of our Suzhou, who specialized in "stealing jade and seducing foreign women" throughout his life, still has so many admirers who pluck the icy strings and "smile" and "smile again" on the radio broadcasting station. The literati salivate over other people's antiques and calligraphy, but have no way to obtain them, so "of the thirty-six strategies, stealing is the best." Even if "both the thief and the stolen goods are caught," it is still a "strong thief's demeanor." Sun Wukong stealing peaches and ginseng fruits is even more eternally famous and immortal.

It can be seen that "stealing" is not "despicable," so the great Mr. Pu, who carried out "stealing the country," may still receive the "duke" title in the future?

But the foreign devils are ultimately useless, unable to catch up with our Chinese "civilized lineage," engaging in secretive activities and specializing in robbery and murder. What they consider the most heroic is "piracy." Whether in novels or movies, the more mercilessly pirates kill, the more they are admired. The "bandits" on land are also admired by all. Therefore, the "Lincheng train robbery" can make people from all countries

jump in fright, and the pirates in Dapeng Bay make foreign devils "vigilant" and dare not underestimate the Chinese, who are a bunch of pus-filled cowards, but also have many "heroes." Therefore, the 108 heroes of Liangshan Marsh, who have always been regarded as "jumping clowns," if someone is full and has nothing to do, might as well translate them into foreign languages and spread them to various countries. Not only can they make a lot of profit, but they can also make the foreign devils who "value robbery over theft" dare not look down on us Chinese again.

However, whether you are a "thief" in front of Chinese people or a "robber" in front of foreigners, you must "know your place." As a thief, you must be "romantic and elegant," or "bold and reckless." As a robber, you must go so far as to "rob merchant ships" or "occupy mountain strongholds." If you steal short shirts and pants or rob silk threads on the road, once you are caught by the officials, although you may get to release your sexual desire once after a certain period, "lying high in an iron window" is ultimately not what you want.

China is Full of Gold 204

— Tu Hongxia

Several hundred years ago, an Italian priest named Matteo Ricci came to China to preach. When he returned, in order to make the people of his country understand the situation in China, he specially wrote a book called "Oriental Inquiries," which described everything about China. In particular, one point was very noticeable, saying: "China is full of gold and jewels." This led people from Europe and the West to come to China in droves to see what it was really like. This was, of course, a disappointing thing.

Unexpectedly, recently, this sentence has actually come true. You can make money everywhere. Airline tickets and champagne tickets are opportunities to make a fortune. The empty cigarette packs left over from smoking can be exchanged for lottery tickets and ingots, and used for foreign money. The wrapping paper and empty boxes left over from using soap can also be exchanged for lottery tickets and foreign money...

From this, we can see that people who are keen on making money, who originally smoked a pack of cigarettes every day, now smoke more and more in order to have more opportunities to make money, gradually increasing to two packs, three packs... Friends who use soap are also quickly using, buying, and exchanging tickets to quickly win prizes, so the shareholders in the company are all smiling with delight and can't close their mouths.

Originally, money is what everyone likes. In China, it is indeed full of gold, and you can make money everywhere. A poor scholar can become rich without lifting a finger.

Mr. Matteo Ricci, thank you for your prediction, which has become a reality. However, is this a good phenomenon? Of course, there is a great deal of reason for this, and I don't need to say more, so I will stop writing here.

Kissing 205

— Xu Xiaoting

When the heat of love between two sexes reaches its peak, they follow it with a kiss in order to seek sexual comfort. On the stage of love, kissing is an unavoidable scene in a play, but from the perspective of hygienists, although kissing between two sexes can provide comfort in love, if one party has an infectious disease, such as syphilis, leprosy, tuberculosis, etc., even though they can enjoy the

right to love between lip and lip contact, they must also taste the obligation of contracting germs. Therefore, although the term "kissing" is so fragrant and flavorful, if you look at it from the other side, there are both advantages and disadvantages!

Kissing between people is direct, and kissing between people and things is

indirect. We know that flies in summer are extremely dirty. Their bodies squat on food, and their saliva remains in the dishes. If we are not careful and eat this kind of food,

there is indeed no difference from kissing flies. The transmission of disease and the loss of life, the price of this kiss, is truly alarming! Eradicating flies in summer is seen by mankind as the most urgent and important task that cannot be delayed. Women and children all understand this principle. Kissing between people and flies is truly a terrible thing!

In addition, there is a matter in society that people do not pay attention to, which is the old newspapers that have been read by people and are regarded as waste. Because people study the utilization of waste, they use them to wrap copper coins and paste walls. However, there is a boss who opens a food store who is really nervous and takes them to wrap food. The writing on the newspapers and the ink used are known to anyone with knowledge to contain toxic

substances, and can only be looked at but not eaten. Now, because of wrapping food, people's mouths can indirectly have intimate kisses with them. This kind of harm is no different from eating the saliva of flies!

From the above points of view, kissing between people is fragrant and flavorful, but it still contains dangerous facts! Kissing between people and things is neither voluntary nor invisible, and the harm obtained is really like a dumb person dreaming of his mother, unable to express the pain! Disasters come from the mouth. We must pay special attention to our daily life and diet, and not carelessly make indirect contact with dangerous things.

Anything that can fly to Lushan without wings

must be a person.

Anyone who lives in a villa and has a car is definitely a rich person.

Anyone who often enters a pawnshop is definitely a poor person.

Anyone with red, blue, black, and white colors on their face is definitely a modern woman.

Anyone who suffers all kinds of humiliation abroad and ends up becoming a displaced overseas Chinese is definitely a Chinese person.

Anyone who receives copper salaries, drives a car, and is incredibly noble in high-level Chinese institutions is definitely a foreigner.

Four Northeast Company Commanders 207

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 15: The Guest Leaves With Bashful Tenderness, Waves With a Smile

Someone Comes to Visit, Old Enmities Start, Sadness is Awakened

Guizhi really had nothing to say, but seeing Zhao Ziqiang in such an awkward state, if she didn't comfort him, she was afraid that this honest man would have other doubts, so she said, "You don't need to say anything, I know all these things. Aren't my ears for listening? Aren't my eyes for seeing?" After saying this, she sighed and smiled again. Zhao Ziqiang saw that her words already carried a hint of joking, as if they were much more familiar, so he said with a smile, "Please don't be polite, eat whatever you want." Guizhi remained silent for a while, and still stood up, looking as if she wanted to leave. Zhao Ziqiang touched his head and smiled, "Is there anything urgent at home?" Guizhi hesitated for a while before smiling, "Although there's nothing urgent, I've been out for too long, and my mother will ask." As she spoke, she had already walked out. Zhao Ziqiang felt that she didn't necessarily have to leave, but he didn't know how to persuade her to stay, so he let her go. Watching Guizhi leave, he couldn't help feeling disappointed, so he couldn't help but follow her from behind. He followed her all the way to the counter, and Guizhi turned around, stopped, and waved her hands at him, saying, "Don't see me off, don't see me off!" When she said this, her brow was slightly furrowed, naturally expressing that she was not very willing. Zhao Ziqiang understood and didn't walk any further. He returned to the booth, paid for the refreshments, and happily walked home. As he passed through the courtyard, the sound of his leather shoes stepping on the floor tiles clearly showed that he was very pleased. He took off his hat with one hand and lifted the cotton curtain with the other, calling out "Dad" and bowing to Zhao Weng. Zhao Weng saw that he was smiling and asked in a low voice, "Did you get any news?" Zhao Ziqiang didn't say anything, but couldn't help but smile, and nodded, "It's probably no problem." Zhao Weng took down the tobacco pipe hanging on his belt, lit it, and slowly smoked it. (185)

Killing a Chicken 208

— Guo Qiushen

My mother wanted to eat chicken. So today, Luo came back from the vegetable market with a yellow hen in her basket. The chicken was bought, but there was no one to kill it. Both Luo and my mother were very timid, and they would tremble when they picked up a knife. My mother had never even killed a fish. According to her, she had never stepped on an ant to death in her life, let alone killed a chicken. Therefore, this murderer was pushed onto me. "Heaven has the virtue of cherishing life, and humans have a heart of compassion." I should not make things difficult for them, so "gentlemen should stay away from the kitchen."

I rolled up my sleeves, held the knife in one hand, and grabbed the chicken's wings, legs, and head together with the other hand. I plucked some of the feathers from the chicken's neck, and just as I was about to put the knife to it, I caught sight of Luo holding Lin beside me. Of course, I told Luo to take Lin away, so that this little pure soul would not be imprinted with this impression of cruel behavior.

Watching the white knife go in and the red knife come out, the chicken's blood flowed gurglingly. After a moment, it closed its eyes tightly. Then I put down the bucket, stretched its legs a few times, and sang out some faint final struggles, and its life was over.

Originally, killing a chicken is a small matter, what does it count as cruel behavior? In this bustling city during the day, people killing people is a common occurrence, and we Chinese are especially like little chickens, being slaughtered by others!

Are we forever being slaughtered!

Small Crafts

Methods for Making Household Soap and Toilet Soap 209

— Yan Chonglou

Soap is an essential daily commodity, generally divided into household soap and toilet soap. Here are the detailed manufacturing methods, for the reference of those interested in practical industries.

The raw materials used for household soap include tallow, rosin, cottonseed oil, soybean oil, tung oil, castor oil, coconut oil, soda ash, lime, etc. First, mix various oils and dissolve them in a ground vat. Then, use a pump to pump them into an acid vat, add sulfuric acid, and after six hours, remove impurities and moisture for later use. Separately, take lime and water, dissolve them in an alkali vat, and gradually add the above-purified oil into the alkali vat, heating it with steam until it becomes milky. The next day, lime soap is formed. Transport the lime soap through a crusher and grinder, and a conveyor to a storage tank above a stainless steel leaching column. Soak it with highly heated water for twelve hours, then release it, which is called "sweet water," and it tastes very sweet! Inject it into an evaporation tank to evaporate the water, then pass it through a leaching machine to obtain crude glycerol, which can be used for other industrial products. Transfer the lime soap in the leaching column, after removing the sweet water, to a soap pot using a conveyor. Simultaneously, add soda ash and heat with steam. After twelve hours, add sodium chloride to separate the soap from the lime. The floating part is the soap, and the sinking part is the lime mud. Release the lime mud and store it in a ground pool. Use water to extract the alkali solution from the lime mud. The remaining lime mud, after drying, becomes crude calcium carbonate, which can be used for industrial products. Heat the extracted alkali solution with rosin using steam to create rosin soap. Mix the rosin soap with the soap in the soap pot, and after twelve hours, pure soap is formed. Then, use a pump to pump it into a soap machine for storage. When ready to use, inject the soap from the soap machine into a mixer, add fragrance, and use a refrigeration pump to pump it into a soap cooling machine. After half an hour, it solidifies into a large block. Then, take it out and use a soap cutting machine to cut it into

small pieces, and household soap is made.

The oils used for toilet soap are slightly different from those for household soap, mainly consisting of tallow, coconut oil, and castor oil. The manufacturing process is also the same as described above for household soap, except that a separate pot is used for boiling. After the soap is formed, it is also injected into a soap cooling machine to solidify into blocks. Then, it is cut into long strips and placed in a glass vacuum room for bleaching. After several months, when it becomes pure white, move it to a spiraling drying room. The upper part of the room has a planing machine. Take the pure white long strips of soap, put them into the planing machine, and plane them into flakes. Use the spiral device to spread them on several layers of copper wire for drying in the room. After about one or two hours, transfer a certain amount of the soap to a soap mixer, add fragrance and pigment, and start the mixer. After about an hour, transfer it to a grinding machine. Repeat this process several times until the fragrance and pigment are thoroughly mixed. Then, transfer it to a spiral extrusion machine. The

inside is like a spiral shaft. The soap is extruded by the spiral, and the product can be changed into various models, so round, square, etc., can be made.

The long strips extruded from the extrusion machine are cut into small pieces using a separator, and then moved to a printing press for printing. Place them in shallow wooden grids and move them to another vacuum drying room. After drying for about a week, toilet

soap is made.

Reporter's Note: The above describes the indirect soap-making method of Mr. Lever Brothers. The Wuzhou Guben Soap Factory, run by Chinese businessmen, uses this method for manufacturing, and its products are of excellent quality! There is no need to elaborate. However, in recent years, foreign goods and inferior soaps have been rampantly manufactured and sold at reduced prices, attempting to dump their products, which is a hidden danger for the future of domestic goods!

Central Propaganda Committee Actively Guides the Film Industry 213

The Central Propaganda Committee believes that the film industry is of great importance and can increase the effectiveness of film propaganda. It has established a Film Industry Guidance Committee to preside over the guidance and design of the national film industry. The organizational outline of the Guidance Committee has been submitted to the Central Government for approval and filing. Chen Guofu, Dai Ce, Guo Youshou, Chen Lifu, Fang Zhi, Shao Yuanchong, Huang Ying, Du Tingxiu, Qian Changzhao, Shen Ruo, He Zhonghan, Liang Naixian, Lin Weiwen, Huang Renlin, and Luo Jialun have been hired as fifteen members to form the committee. The organizational outline of the Film Industry Guidance Committee of the Central Propaganda Committee is

copied below: (1) This committee is organized by the Central Propaganda Committee. (2) The scope of work of this committee is as follows: A. Guide the national film industry to promote film propaganda work. B. Design matters related to film propaganda for adoption by the Central Propaganda Committee. C. Matters submitted by the Central Propaganda Committee for research. (3) This committee has fifteen members, the director and deputy director of the Propaganda Committee are ex officio members, and the rest are appointed by the Central Propaganda Committee. (4) This committee selects three to five standing committee members from the Central Propaganda Committee to preside over all committee affairs. (5) This committee has one secretary, who handles daily affairs under the order of the standing committee. (6) The results of the research or suggestions of this committee are sent to the Central Propaganda Committee for

selection and implementation. (7) This committee should make a general report to the Central Propaganda Committee once a month. (8) This committee should hold a meeting at least once a week, but when necessary, a temporary meeting may be held, convened by the standing committee. (9) The standing committee members take turns as chairmen when this committee meets. (10) All members of this committee are voluntary. (11) This committee may employ staff according to the complexity of the affairs, and negotiate with the Central Propaganda Committee to transfer and use them. (12) If there are any matters not covered in this outline, this committee may propose to the Central

Propaganda Committee to amend it. (13) This outline is submitted to the Central Standing Committee for filing and implementation after approval by the Central Propaganda

Committee.

Hangzhou Normal School Promotes Elementary Education Correspondence School 215

The Extension Education Office of the Provincial Hangzhou Normal School, in order to provide elementary school teachers in various places with opportunities for further study and increase educational effectiveness, hired experts from various fields last semester to run elementary education correspondence classes. Participants included counties and cities in this province, as well as provinces such as Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Hunan, Hubei, Guangdong, Jiangxi, Fujian, Anhui, Sichuan, and Jiangsu. Later, due to the limited number of places, many teachers from distant places were unable to join. During the summer vacation, they also sent letters requesting it. It is now heard that the school has continued to recruit 500 new students. All courses, such as children's literature, training issues, labor education, singing and teaching, and Chinese, arithmetic, social studies, nature, and other teaching methods, are extremely practical. Local News

Shanghai Municipal Elementary School Teacher Certification Method Filed by the Ministry of Education 216

(Nanjing News) The Ministry of Education recently issued document No. 677, in reply to the Shanghai Municipal Government, regarding the regulations for the certification of elementary school teachers in the city, stating that it should be renamed "Provisional Measures," and that the rest of the content is in order and approved for filing. The entire method is recorded below:

Article 1. The certification of elementary school teachers in this city shall be handled in accordance with these regulations until the Ministry of Education promulgates the regulations for the certification of elementary school teachers. Article 2. The elementary school education certification in this city is divided into two types: certification without examination and certification with examination. Article 3. Anyone who possesses one of the following qualifications and wishes to serve as an elementary school educator in this city shall be subject to certification without examination: 1. Graduated from a old-style middle school or higher, and has served as an elementary school teacher for more than one year, or has attended summer school education courses offered by local educational administrative agencies or university education colleges and normal schools for two summer sessions; 2. Graduated from a two-year or more normal training course or simple normal school simple normal course, and has served as an elementary school teacher for more than two years or has attended the above-mentioned summer school for three summer sessions; 3. Has served as an elementary school teacher for more than three years and has been recognized by the educational administrative agency as having definite achievements, or has attended the above-mentioned summer school for four summer sessions; 4. Has served as an elementary school teacher for more than three years and has published a special work on elementary school education, which has been recognized by this bureau as having definite value. Article 4. Anyone who possesses one of the following qualifications and wishes to serve as an elementary school teacher in this city shall be subject to certification with examination: 1. Has graduated from a old-style middle school or senior high school; 2. Has studied at a normal school or senior high school for one year and has served as an elementary school teacher for more than one year; 3. Has attended a

Normal training course, simple normal school, or simple normal course; 4. Has been an elementary school teacher for more than three years; 5. Has special expertise and has been an elementary school teacher for more than one year. Article 5. Those who are certified as qualified may serve as class teachers or specialist teachers, and their qualifications shall be determined by reviewing their certificates or examination results. Article 6. Those who are to be certified shall register with this bureau and fill out various forms at the time of registration, and submit two recent half-length photos of themselves, together with the required supporting documents for verification. Article 7. The date and location of registration and certification shall be announced by this bureau in the newspaper. Article 8. Certification without examination shall be decided after passing a physical examination and reviewing various certificates (diplomas, certificates of study, certificates of service, and works). Examination and certification are divided into three items: physical examination, written examination, and oral examination. Those who fail the physical examination may not take the written or oral examination. Article 9. The subjects for the written examination for certification are as follows: A. The subjects for the written examination for class teachers are: (1) Party Principles, (2) Chinese, (3) Arithmetic, (4) General Knowledge, (5) Education. B. The subjects for the written examination for specialist teachers are: (1) Party Principles, (2) Chinese, (3) General Knowledge, (4) Education, (5) Specialist Subject. Article 10. Those who pass the certification shall be issued a certificate of certification by this bureau. Article 11. The validity period of the certificate of certification is set at three years. Article 12. These regulations may be revised at any time if there are any matters not covered. Article 13. These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Shanghai Municipal Middle and Elementary School Examination Failure Remedial Measures 217

Approved by the Ministry of Education

(Nanjing News) The Ministry of Education has issued Instruction No. 9104 for the Shanghai Municipal Government's proposed remedial measures for students who fail one or two subjects in the middle and elementary school graduation examinations. Except for the amendment of Article 7, the rest are approved for filing. The full text of the measures is recorded below:

1. Students who participate in the graduation examination of middle and elementary schools in this city and fail one or two subjects, and fail again after the re-examination, should take remedial classes in the subjects they failed according to the provisions of these measures. 2. The location of the remedial classes for remedial students should be determined by themselves, either in the original school, another school, or outside the school. 3. If remedial students go to another school for remedial classes, they should obtain the consent of the other school and ask the original school to issue the student's academic record and the grades of the subjects that need remedial classes, along with a half-length photo, and send it to the remedial school. 4. For the second semester of the 21st year, students who fail one subject after the re-examination in subjects other than Chinese, Foreign Language, Arithmetic, Physics, and Chemistry in the high school examination will be issued a certificate by this bureau and allowed to apply for colleges and universities first. After being admitted, they will be probationary students and should continue to take remedial classes in the subjects they failed and participate in the next examination. 5. Students in junior high school and elementary school who need remedial classes may listen to applicants with equivalent academic qualifications, but

may not be promoted with graduation qualifications. 6. Remedial students, whether they take remedial classes in the original school or another school, should pay tuition and miscellaneous fees according to ordinary students, but the school should reduce the fees for textbooks and other fees appropriately. 7. Students taking remedial classes in the original school or another school, if they are day students, should go to the school for remedial classes in the subjects they failed in the examination during the prescribed time, and should go home for self-study during the rest of the time. If they are boarding students, they should review their homework in the self-study room during other class times in addition to attending classes in the remedial subjects, and must abide by all the rules of the school. 8. Remedial students may apply to the Education Bureau through the remedial school to participate in the next examination for the subjects they failed when this city holds the next examination, but only once. Remedial students outside the school should apply to the Education Bureau through the original school to participate in the next examination for the subjects they failed, but only once. 9. These measures shall be implemented after being filed with the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government.

Overview of Blind and Deaf Education in This City 219

A total of one school for the blind and four schools for the deaf and mute.

All are elementary schools; secondary schools lack qualified teachers.

Blind and deaf education is a special form of education. China, with its blind and deaf population accounting for one-thousandth of the national population, urgently needs active development in this area. Recognizing this, the Ministry of Education recently issued orders to the education departments of various provinces and cities to investigate the overall situation of blind and deaf education nationwide as a reference for research and to seek pathways for development. Shanghai has witnessed irregular development in education at all levels, from elementary to higher education, but few have paid attention to this special education. To understand the status of blind and deaf education in this city, the reporter made separate visits to various schools for the blind and deaf yesterday. The findings are recorded as follows for the reference of those concerned about blind and deaf education.

One School for the Blind: There were originally two schools for the blind in this city. One was affiliated with the Qunxue Society, founded before the January 28th Incident, with only three students. After one semester, it was suspended due to the January 28th Incident and has not been reopened. The other was founded by a British person on Yidingpan Road, with Fu Lanya as the principal. The number of students is minimal, and the school is not thriving.

Shanghai School for the Deaf and Mute: This school was newly established this semester, located on Zhaojia Road, Ximen. The school board includes Chen Heqin, Zhang Shouyong, and Ou Yuanhuai, among others. The principal is Sun Yusen. Currently, there are five teachers and seventy-five students, making it the most dynamic school for the deaf and mute in this city. Yesterday, the reporter visited the school and was led on a tour by teacher Shi Dianqing. The student dormitory was exceptionally clean, and the classrooms included one each for primary and advanced levels. Various statistical charts were quite detailed. Under Sun's guidance, students demonstrated pronunciation and sign language to the reporter, which was quite interesting. One student, Sun Kerun, had been trained at the Yantai School for the Deaf and Mute for three years and transferred to this school this semester. He speaks like a normal person. The student read the school's regulations to the reporter with clear pronunciation, which was truly remarkable.

Affiliated with Qunxue Society: The school for the deaf and mute affiliated with the Qunxue Society on Zhonghua Road was founded in April of the Republic of China year nine. At that time, it was the only school for the deaf and mute founded by Chinese people. The Municipal Education Bureau subsidizes its expenses with

one hundred yuan per month. Yang Pingyu is the principal. Last semester, there were ninety students, but this semester, the number has decreased to twenty-seven. There are a total of three teachers. The school previously established a vocational program at the junior high level but has now discontinued it. Seven students have graduated, some of whom have become teachers at schools for the deaf and mute, while others work as typists, all contributing to society.

Founded by Foreigners: There are two other schools, one being the Fu Lanya School for the Deaf and Mute on Jisifei Road, established by a British person in September of the Republic of China year fifteen. Fu Lanya is the principal, and there are currently fifty-five students. Another school is the School for the Deaf and Mute attached to the Xujiahui Notre Dame Convent, established by the French Catholic Church. Fei Mumu is the principal, and there are currently twenty-seven students. Founded nine years before the Republic of China, it is the most historically long-standing school for the deaf and mute in this city.

General Survey of the Deaf and Mute: In addition to the four schools in Shanghai, there are more than ten schools for the deaf and mute nationwide, including those in Yantai, Beiping, Nantong, Nanjing, Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Zhenjiang. The number of students is approximately four hundred. Although there are no accurate statistics on the number of deaf and mute people nationwide, it is generally estimated that they account for one in every thousand people, totaling as many as 400,000. The causes of deafness and muteness are said to be 60% direct inheritance, 24% indirect inheritance, 12% consanguineous marriage, and 4% ear diseases during speech development.

Severe Shortage of Teachers: According to Mr. Shi of the Shanghai School for the Deaf and Mute, the main reasons why deaf and mute education in China cannot develop are, first, the lack of school funding, and second, the lack of qualified teachers, with the latter being even more critical than the former. In the past, only the Yantai School for the Deaf and Mute established a normal school class, and nothing similar has been heard of elsewhere. Therefore, schools for the deaf and mute in China only have elementary schools, and it is difficult to establish vocational programs at the junior high level or above. It is deeply hoped that the educational community will pay attention to this point.

One of the "Shen Bao" Series: "Japanese Aviation" Publication 220

The development of the world's aviation industry in recent times is astonishing. The "Air Age" is approaching step by step. Japan is currently working hard to enrich and expand its air force, encourage and assist the civil aviation industry, and vigorously revitalize the aviation industry, reversing its previous weakness and showing a trend of surpassing Europe and the United States. Mr. Xu Yuanruo has specially compiled this book for the reference of the Chinese people. The book consists of five chapters, detailing the past, present, and future of Japanese aviation, Japanese air defense, the trans-Pacific problem, juvenile airmen, and other aviation

business, exercises, and other current situations. The content is rich and detailed, and the text is shocking. Recently, the Chinese people have gradually become interested in aviation, and this book is the best reading material to meet this need. The actual price is 25 cents, and it is published by the special distribution department of this newspaper. A special price is offered for one month during the autumn school season. Purchases of ten or more copies are calculated at a 30% discount.

Third China Vocational Supplementary School 221

Five departments to be established first... A good opportunity for young people to pursue further education. The China Vocational Education Society previously established the First and Second Supplementary Schools in the concession areas to promote supplementary education, with excellent results. Now, the Third China Vocational Supplementary School is established within the China Vocational School at Lujiabang, Xiaoximen. It will initially offer five departments: mechanical and electrical engineering, architectural and civil engineering drawing, added engineering, Chinese language and writing, and English. Classes are all taught in the evening. Among them, there is a particularly high demand in society for talents in the fields of mechanical and electrical engineering and architectural and civil engineering drawing. The establishment of these two departments by the school not only meets the needs

but is also an innovation among supplementary schools in the country. Moreover, the China Vocational School has complete facilities, such as the mechanical workshop, prime mover testing laboratory, electrical laboratory, and civil engineering research room, all of which are richly equipped. It is said that the existing equipment will be used to provide practical training and testing for supplementary students. It is also heard that the school will start soon, and registrations have been very enthusiastic. Those who request the prospectus should enclose two cents for postage.

Alumni of Nanyang Advanced Business School Petition the Ministry of Education to Commend Wu Xinglian 224

Last Saturday evening (August 26th), alumni of the Nanyang Advanced Business School in this city held the fourth alumni reunion dinner at the YMCA in the French Concession, with a large number of attendees. After the dinner, alumni Yang Yingcong and others proposed that Principal Wu Xinglian founded Nanyang Business School in the Republic of China year nine, sacrificing his family wealth to do so, for fourteen years. During the January 28th Incident, the entire school was destroyed, with significant losses. Not only was Principal Wu not discouraged by this, but he also worked harder to continue the school, gradually restoring it to its former glory in less than a year. Moreover, he has been stationed at the school year-round, focusing on education, handling all matters, big and small, personally, correcting the modern malpractice of nominal principals. Therefore, they initiated a joint petition to the Ministry of Education for commendation. Yesterday, Lou Weitao, a graduate of the first class of the school, submitted the petition, which was signed and sealed by all the alumni, directly to the Ministry of Education in the capital, requesting appropriate commendation in accordance with the regulations on commending individuals who donate funds to establish schools and the regulations on lifelong education service.

Renovation of the Baseball Field into a Hospital Has Not Been Formally Approved 228

Rockefeller Foundation to Hold a Meeting in November

Site Reception Needs to Be Postponed to Next Year

Rockefeller, the American oil tycoon, previously agreed to the request of the Chinese Red Cross Hospital and others to donate the land of the Chinese baseball field on Jin Shenfu Road in Shanghai, worth more than three million yuan, to rebuild the Zhongshan Hospital. The Chinese side entrusted Yan Fuqing, the president of the Red Cross Hospital, to take charge of the matter, actively planning and raising funds. The construction was originally scheduled to begin in August or September after autumn. According to Mr. Fang, although the proposal has been approved by Rockefeller, it has not yet been formally approved by the Rockefeller Foundation Committee in New York. The committee was originally scheduled to meet in August of this year but has now been rescheduled to November. Therefore, the formal reception of the site will have to wait until after November, and the construction date will also have to be changed slightly, probably starting in the spring of next year. As for the funding, it is planned to raise one million yuan, and 500,000 yuan has already been raised, with considerable arrangements for the remaining amount. The Rockefeller Foundation will also formally send a letter notifying the relocation of the baseball field.

Schedule for the Hong Kong Chinese Volleyball Team's Matches in Shanghai 232

Four Matches Scheduled

But the Fourteenth is Undecided

The Hong Kong volleyball champion Chinese volleyball team, a group of nine people, arrived in Shanghai by boat the day before yesterday and stayed at the Hongkou Grand Hotel. They plan to compete with various strong teams in Shanghai to learn from each other. The Association has arranged the schedule with various teams, as follows. However, the opponent for the match on the fourteenth has not yet been found. Those who wish to compete with them should contact Zhou Jiaqi before 6 PM today. The schedule is listed below:

Fourteenth 4:00 PM vs. Undecided

Sixteenth 4:00 PM vs. Daxia

Nineteenth 4:00 PM vs. Fudan

Moore Basketball Team Defeats Youyou 233

The Moore basketball team played a friendly match with Youyou last night, and Moore won with a score of 37-32. Tonight, Moore will compete with the Jingwu A team.

Announcement by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau 234

Competition Regulations for the Municipal Games (Continued from Yesterday)

Article IX: Volleyball Championship

(1) The number of registered team members for each team is limited to twelve for both men and women.

(2) Each match will be a best-of-five-game system.

(3) The competition will use a knockout system, and the order will be drawn by the competition department. The winner of the final will receive the championship.

(4) The competition rules will be implemented in accordance with the latest men's and women's volleyball rules revised and approved by the China National Sports Association.

Article X: Baseball Championship

(1) The number of registered team members for each team is limited to fifteen.

(2) Each match will be nine innings to determine the winner, but it can be changed with the consent of both parties.

(3) The competition will use a knockout system, and the order will be drawn by the competition department. The winner of the final will receive the championship.

(4) The competition rules will be implemented in accordance with the latest baseball rules revised and approved by the National Games in the Republic of China year twenty-two.

Article XI: Softball Championship

(1) The number of registered team members for each team is limited to fifteen.

(2) Each match will be nine innings to determine the winner, but it can be changed with the consent of both parties.

(3) The competition will use a knockout system, and the order will be drawn by the competition department. The final victor

will be awarded the championship.

(4) The competition rules will be implemented in accordance with the most recent softball regulations reviewed and approved by the National Games of the Republic of China in the twenty-second year.

Article XII: Participation Method

(1) Each athlete should fill in the sports events they are participating in and other necessary information in detail on the various athlete registration forms prepared by the Association and send them to the Association before the date specified in the announcement.

(2) Each athlete should send the registration forms by registered mail or other proper methods, sending them with sufficient time before the deadline. Late or incomplete forms will not be accepted.

(3) All athlete registration forms must be filled in clearly with black ink using the forms prepared by the Association for easy compilation, review, and future statistics. Forms using self-prepared paper that do not follow the format or are not filled in clearly will be considered invalid.

(4) If a registered athlete cannot attend the competition temporarily due to an unforeseen reason (such as discovering that the qualification is not met or other unavoidable accidents), they may apply in writing for a replacement before the date specified in the announcement. The replacement athlete must still have a formal registration form, and no changes will be allowed after the deadline.

Article XIII: Protests

(1) Disputes over the competition, such as those stipulated in the rules that the referee's

ruling shall be final, may not be protested.

(2) A legal protest during the competition should first be made orally at the time of the incident and then formally submitted to the jury in writing, signed and sealed, within two hours.

(3) Protests regarding the qualifications of athletes should be submitted to the jury for resolution using the same procedures as above, along with the facts of the disqualification or other evidence.

(4) A formal written protest shall be accompanied by a security deposit of five yuan. If the jury deems the protest to be unfounded, it may be forfeited.

Article XIV: Disciplinary Actions

(1) Athletes participating in the pentathlon, decathlon, swimming, and tennis competitions who are not qualified shall have their competition qualifications immediately revoked upon verification, as well as the scores and prizes they have already obtained or should have obtained.

(2) If any of the team members participating in the football, basketball, volleyball, baseball, or softball competitions are not qualified, the team's competition qualification in that championship shall be immediately revoked upon verification, as well as the scores and prizes they have already obtained or should have obtained.

(3) In the two cases mentioned above, if it is discovered after the closing ceremony, the scores and prizes obtained may still be pursued and taken back in accordance with the law, and severe disciplinary action shall be taken.

(4) Any athlete who lacks competitive spirit during the competition, engages in improper behavior, fails to observe order, disregards public morality, insults other athletes or staff, or disobeys fair referees shall be subject to appropriate punishment by the referees and jury at any time.

Article XV: Awards

(1) Individuals or groups who win various championships will be given various prizes by the Association to show honor.

(2) The top four winners of each event will be given medals of various grades by the Association as a memento. Members of the championship team in ball games will be given medals according to the first place.

(3) Track and field and swimming athletes who can create new records in this city will be given special prizes by the Association to encourage them.

Article XVI: Supplementary Provisions

(1) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be revised at any time. (2) These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation by the Education Bureau.
